Economic Conference Situation Serious Under Currency War Control 31

French Representative Submits an Ultimatum

If Currency Is Not Stabilized Soon

They Will Propose That the Conference Be Adjourned Indefinitely

Chairman Cables President Roosevelt 32

Requesting Swift Adoption of Measures to Stabilize the Dollar

European Gold Bloc Forms United Front Against the United States 33

London This morning, the activities of the World Economic Conference were completely controlled by the sharp rise and fall of currency values. Professor Moley, President Roosevelt's trusted advisor, began his activities today and discussed the issue of currency stability with the US delegation. The delegations of other countries also held meetings, the main one being the meeting of the European gold standard countries. The British delegation, led by MacDonald and Chamberlain, is making every effort to coordinate the opinions of all parties. However, they now feel that declaring the pound's link to gold will isolate the United States and the economic conference will collapse as a whole. Furthermore, the gold standard countries are deeply concerned that the pound's value will be lowered by the dollar. If this happens, the commerce of the gold standard countries will be severely negatively impacted. The currency issue is currently stalled, and much of the conference's work has actually been suspended as a result. The US delegation has not yet been involved in formal discussions, but they are being informed of the progress at all times. According to recent news, French Finance Minister Bonnet will propose that if a compromise on currency stability cannot be reached within a week, the conference should be adjourned. It is said that there is some basis for this statement. MacDonald met with Hull again today, urging him to pay attention to the seriousness of the situation. It is rumored that the US delegation has cabled President Roosevelt, suggesting that he take all appropriate measures as soon as he deems appropriate. However, the authorities subsequently issued a denial. At the same time, Cox, chairman of the Monetary and Financial Committee, reiterated his refusal to discuss currency stability and advised Europeans to find their own solutions. (29th Reuters Telegram)

London Those seeking general currency stability at the World Economic Conference are now greatly alarmed by the rapid decline of the dollar. The representatives of the European gold standard countries, while claiming to support the gold standard, surrounded British Prime Minister MacDonald, seeking British assistance. However, they achieved nothing other than obtaining Prime Minister's promise to give preferential attention. The British government seems unwilling to take sides in the conflict between the United States and the European gold standard countries, and is even less willing to take any action given the dollar's wild fluctuations. (29th Reuters Telegram)

London France has effectively issued an ultimatum to the economic conference, warning that if a currency stabilization agreement cannot be reached within a week, the French representative will propose an indefinite adjournment. However, while France has issued an ultimatum, Britain also tends to join the European gold standard countries, while the United States still adheres to its original policy, refusing to participate in any stabilization agreement at this time.

The French ultimatum was sent to Conference Chairman MacDonald. It is said that the gold standard defense alliance of all major countries and other allied countries such as Italy, Belgium, the Netherlands, and Switzerland all agreed to this move during repeated private talks.

This afternoon, it was learned that the French ultimatum was sent out yesterday. As a result, the US representatives reiterated their stance of refusing to stabilize the currency today. As a result, everyone at the conference looked worried, because they had previously speculated that the US dollar's sharp decline might mean that the US President had considered stabilizing the currency, but they did not expect the US representatives to still make a statement of rejection.

Representatives of the gold standard countries, such as French Finance Minister Bonnet, Belgian Foreign Minister Hymans, and representatives from Switzerland, Italy, and the Netherlands, held a secret meeting this morning. They then met with British Prime Minister MacDonald and Finance Minister Chamberlain. However, both meetings failed to produce concrete results. French Finance Minister Bonnet told reporters after meeting with British representatives that he had not made any progress, but said that they would meet again this afternoon. US representatives told reporters after hearing the news of the French ultimatum that today was the darkest day of the conference. The representatives of the six major countries who had originally planned to draft a currency plan after the United States refused to reconsider its policy on stabilization were also postponed, as it was felt that it would be useless to continue discussing a plan to prevent currency fluctuations at this time. This afternoon, it was widely rumored in the conference lounge that British Prime Minister MacDonald had sent a personal letter to President Roosevelt, urging him to take steps to stabilize the US dollar as soon as possible within the possible scope of the conference. It is now believed that this extraordinary move by the British Prime Minister was the result of France's reiteration of the ultimatum it sent yesterday this morning. It was also heard that during this morning's meeting of gold standard countries, Belgian representative Francqui was the most激烈, declaring that unless the Belgians were assisted in maintaining the gold standard, Belgium would have no choice but to withdraw from the conference. In addition, other representatives also expressed that they urgently needed to return to their countries to deal with the increasingly critical financial situation. However, Britain is now firmly leaning towards the gold standard countries. The British delegation sent a letter to the conference secretariat last night, strongly advocating the need to curb monetary speculation and fluctuations.

As for the US statement of no change in its attitude towards the stabilization issue, it was issued after US Undersecretary of State Moley met with US delegation advisor, renowned financier Warburg, and US Treasury Department advisor Sprague for two hours. According to a spokesman for the US delegation, there is no prospect of the US dollar being stabilized in the near future, but he acknowledged that Sprague may submit a new plan to the US President during his term. (29th Kuomintang News Agency)

London The World Economic Conference has effectively come to a standstill, awaiting two important statements so that the conference can make real progress.

One is the plan on Australia's stabilization of world wheat prices. It is said that the Australian government has already issued instructions, but the Australian delegation is keeping it secret. It is believed that its contents should provide some kind of plan to reduce the acreage of cultivation, but it is said that the nature of the proposal is quite lenient, so that wheat farmers will not suffer more difficulties, and it is attached with several necessary reservations. If European wheat producing countries cannot implement the same harmony, Australia can protect its own interests. The other is to expect the US delegation to make a statement on stabilizing currency, so that Europe will not have to engage in an exchange rate war with the United States. (29th Kuomintang News Agency)

Continued Decline of the US Dollar Promotes European United Front 34

London Recently, the continued decline of the US dollar has caused great panic among Britain and some countries that have gained trade benefits by depreciating their currencies, fearing that they will suffer significant losses. Therefore, the French delegation seized the opportunity to win over Britain, proposing to stabilize the exchange rate between gold pounds and francs first, so as to form a European united front against the United States. Last night, there were various proposals to induce Britain to join the European currency plan, and there were also requests for Britain to support the gold standard countries. Judging from the current situation, many believe that if Britain is willing to use its stable pound fund to support the franc, the Bank of France will be able to assist the Dutch currency. In this way, the currencies of major European countries can be stabilized on a more flexible basis and prevent the dollar from falling again. The US delegation has not yet expressed any opinion on these proposals, while the French delegation firmly believes that no substantial agreement can be reached on any economic or monetary issue until the United States agrees to some kind of stabilization plan. (29th Kuomintang News Agency)

Inducing Britain to Join the European Group 35

Britain's Attitude Wavering and Cautious

London The only significant developments at today's economic conference are two: one is the extreme pessimism of the French delegation, claiming that the conference has failed to reach any unconditional agreement even within the smallest of subcommittees; the other is the shape of a fierce exchange rate war between Europe and the United States. Major representatives all said that unless US Undersecretary of State Moley can maintain his reputation as an "extraordinary person," Britain will be induced to stabilize the prices of the gold pound and various European gold standard currencies, thereby forcing the United States to accept the de facto stabilization of currencies, as the instability of the US currency has brought the economic conference to a standstill. However, as of today, Britain is still wavering, and it has not yet been decided whether to support US monetary policy or join the European group and agree on the exchange rate between the pound, the Dutch guilder, and the franc. However, today's sharp decline in the US dollar has forced Britain to make a decision, as industrialists are generally panicked by the rapid disappearance of the trade benefits they gained after depreciating the pound. (29th Kuomintang News Agency)

Therefore, domestic and international programs must be considered together. The gradual recovery of the United States is indeed a fact, and it has an ordinary and real component. Yan Huiqing Delivers a Broadcast Speech

(London) Chinese representative Dr. Yan Huiqing delivered a radio broadcast today entitled "China's Importance in the World Economy," which was listened to with great attention. Dr. Yan said that China deeply feels the urgent need for a new era of industrialization and needs large quantities of metals and machinery to develop China's latent wealth. China is a fertile ground for daring investors. Those who are prepared to assist China in economic activities will be rewarded. The British economic survey mission to China in 1930 has stated that China's foreign trade can be increased to the same level as India, which can increase world foreign trade by 300 million pounds per year. However, which Western countries will achieve this result with their vision and enterprising spirit? This is the question. China is a silver using country, but most of its imports come from gold using countries, and importers feel unable to maintain the amount of imports. China has to remit gold due to foreign debts and reparations. At this point, Dr. Yan listed figures to show the serious impact of unstable silver prices and economic instability on China, and said that any plan that can stabilize and raise silver prices will increase China's purchasing power and promote its demand for machinery and cotton textiles. The Chinese delegation fully agrees with the British representative's opinion at the World Economic Conference that the greatest need today is to raise world prices and stabilize the currencies of various countries. Japan Attacks Britain and India's Exclusion of Goods Adhering to the Principle of Freedom of Commerce 43

(London) Japanese representative Ambassador Matsudaira argued in the commercial policy subcommittee of the Economic and Trade Committee on the 28th for the unconditional application of the most-favored-nation clause, indirectly attacking the attitude of the British and Indian governments in excluding Japanese goods. Matsudaira said that Japan's tariff rate is very low compared to other countries, and there is no hindrance to international trade. Japan has always adhered to the principle of free trade and has tried its best to eliminate economic nationalism. In this position, Japan hopes that the economic conference will achieve international cooperation on economic and financial matters. Japan believes that the most regrettable thing is that a certain country (referring to Britain) raised tariffs before and after the opening of the economic conference, violating the fundamental spirit of the conference. This attitude hinders international trade. Japan believes that the early removal of such trade barriers is the fundamental spirit of this conference. However, a method of raising tariffs uniformly in all countries is beneficial to countries with high tariff rates and detrimental to countries with low tariff rates. Japan cannot agree to this method. (28th Jiji News Agency)

There Is No Shortage of Supporters for Raising Silver Prices Mexican Representative Issues Declaration 44

(London) Amid the gold standard's agitation of the whole conference, the issue of silver still has no shortage of supporters. Today, the Mexican representative issued a declaration, arguing for the necessity of fully using silver as an auxiliary monetary standard and establishing an international monetary system to raise prices. However, due to the large number of opponents to the bimetallic system, it is also considered impractical, and it is proposed that silver should not be treated as merely a commodity, as France advocates, but should be completely handled by the Monetary Committee, and the Economic Committee should not interfere. (29th Kuomintang News Agency)

Monetary Treatment Subcommittee Holds Meeting Pittman Amendment Passed 45

(London) Apart from the second subcommittee of the Monetary Committee, all committees of the World Economic Conference held closed-door meetings today. The second subcommittee considered its proposals on the use of gold and the percentage of gold reserves. The BIS's Ley said today that this subcommittee aims to promote the restoration of the gold standard as the international monetary standard. The Monetary Committee discussed the amended text or alternative clauses of the Pittman Amendment at today's closed-door meeting. This new clause was passed after slight word modifications, stating that gold is not required for domestic circulation in modern situations, but only as a reserve for central bank liabilities and to meet foreign claims arising from imbalances in foreign accounts. Therefore, there is no need to inject gold coins or gold notes into domestic circulation. Another clause states that the gold reserves of central banks should have greater flexibility, but a ratio of 25% should be regarded as a sufficient minimum. When the above clauses were debated, Ley advocated passage. Egyptian representative Cooke said that some countries, especially small countries, have a concept that gold has an absolute value. For the future, gold must be regarded as a measure of value, not as a valuable item. (28th Reuters Telegram)

Ministry of Industry Requests Ministry of Finance to Amend Customs Tariffs 50

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Industry believes that many of the tariff rates for various goods stipulated in the current tariff regulations do not conform to the actual situation. For example, raw silk, tung oil, soybean oil, soybean cake, porcelain, and livestock by-products, which are sold abroad in large quantities, are subject to export taxes equal to or higher than those of ordinary products. On the other hand, the import tariff rates for industrial products that are scarce domestically, such as lead blocks and iron wire, exceed those of finished products. All of these factors hinder the development of domestic industry and urgently need to be revised. Therefore, based on the principle of tariff protection policy, a plan for increasing, decreasing, or exempting tariffs has been drafted, requesting the Ministry of Finance to consider amending the current import and export tariffs. Wuhan River Water Begins to Recede 52

Yesterday, It Receded Two Inches, Still Four Inches Above the Levee

Water Levels in Upstream Ports are Receding, Situation Has Eased

(Hankou) The river water receded two inches on the 29th, with the water level at 47 feet, marking the first day of receding water after the monsoon flood. However, it is still four inches above the levee. Water levels in upstream ports are receding, and the situation has eased. (Special Dispatch, 29th)

(Hankou) Several sections of the riverside road in Wuchang have collapsed due to prolonged water immersion and soil erosion. The Provincial Capital Construction Office has dispatched workers to repair them urgently. The Jiujiao embankment in Baishazhou has been reinforced. The Zhoujiazui sluice gate is still not out of danger. Furthermore, the main embankment on the south bank of the Yangtze River has only a few inches of freeboard, creating an extremely dangerous situation. Li Eqi, an inspector from the Provincial Government Disaster Prevention Agency, telegraphed the county chiefs of Wujiajianpu on the 29th, urging them to supervise laborers to carry out rescue work. (Special Dispatch, 29th)

(Hankou) The water level in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River receded significantly on the 29th. Chongqing was at 28 feet on the 29th, a decrease of 3 feet 9 inches from the 28th. Yichang was at 28 feet, a decrease of 6 inches. Yuezhou was at 45 feet, a decrease of 5 inches. Changsha was at 22 feet 3 inches, a decrease of 6 inches. (Central News Agency, 29th)

(Nanjing) The Yangtze River Waterway Improvement Commission announced the water levels at various locations along the Yangtze River on the 29th as follows: (1) Upstream: Chongqing 27.5 feet, 4.2 feet lower than the 28th; Wanxian 48.5 feet, 1.2 feet higher than the 28th; Yichang 26.0 feet, 0.6 feet lower than the 28th; Shashi 21.8 feet, 0.8 feet lower than the 28th. (2) Midstream: Yuezhou 47.0 feet, 0.5 feet lower than the 28th; Hankou 47.2 feet, no change from the 28th; Anqing not detailed; Wuhu 27.6 feet, 0.1 feet higher than the 28th. (3) Downstream: Nanjing 21.7 feet, no change; Zhenjiang 17.9 feet, 0.5 feet lower than the 28th. (Central News Agency, 29th)

(Nanjing) Song Xishang, Director of the Engineering Department of the Yangtze River Waterway Improvement Commission, is scheduled to travel to Xun by boat on the morning of the 30th, accompanied by technical personnel from the commission, to assist in the flood control work along the Yangtze River. Yongding River Rises Again 54

Breaches at Doudian and Liuliudian

(Beiping) According to the Yongding River Works Bureau, due to continuous overcast and rainy weather, the river's water level suddenly rose again. Unexpectedly, there was heavy rain last night, and the water level rose sharply to 15 feet this morning, 5.5 feet higher than before. If the water level continues to rise, the future is worrying. The river has now been assigned special personnel to guard it in sections, and there are no immediate signs of danger. (Special Dispatch, 29th)

(Beiping) The Yongding River breached at Doudian and Liuliudian on the 28th and 29th. Negotiations to Continue Separately After the Disarmament Conference Adjourns 80

Havas, Geneva, 29th: The General Committee of the Disarmament Conference discussed the issue of adjourning the Disarmament Conference this morning. Chairman Henderson explained the necessity of adjournment, stating that negotiations are already underway in London, and that certain points of contention may be difficult to resolve through diplomatic channels. Some delegations believe that adjournment is equivalent to ending the conference. The chairman strongly defended the decision, stating that the conference will continue its work, but in a more appropriate form to achieve success. German delegate Nadolny spoke at length, stating that Germany is prepared to negotiate in London, and declared that the obligations of the Disarmament Conference should be to re-examine the British disarmament plan and negotiate with the various delegations in Geneva, as Chairman Henderson's travels make it difficult to discuss methods. Nadolny expressed regret for the Bureau's decision to adjourn the Disarmament Conference until October 16, stating that the people cannot understand the decision to adjourn, as it is tantamount to abandoning the disarmament mission and declaring the Disarmament Conference dead. He also stated that the governments that approve this decision should bear full responsibility, while Germany will continue to do its utmost to avoid the cessation of the Disarmament Conference. U.S. representative Wilson supported Chairman Henderson's proposal to adjourn, while British representative Cadogan also supported the procedure proposed by the Bureau. French representative Massigli stated that although his personal wishes were not the same, he still accepted the Bureau's proposal, and that the urgent task at hand is to find new methods of working. In response to German representative Nadolny's statement on government responsibility, Massigli stated that in the current situation, governments must consider carefully in order to fully understand the reasons for this serious decision, which is clear to everyone. He also stated that public opinion knows that if all countries are willing to cooperate peacefully, the outcome of whether the Disarmament Conference is adjourned or not will be the same, as no situation should be created anywhere that is contrary to the spirit proposed in Geneva. In short, the responsibility for the failure of the Disarmament Conference can only be determined later when Henderson consults separately with the governments of various countries. At that time, if there is any obstacle to the success of these consultations, there will be no escaping responsibility. Hungary supported Germany's proposal, while Italy supported adjournment. German delegate Nadolny rose again to speak, stating that the General Assembly's discussions cannot change his belief. He represented his government in advocating for the drafting of a disarmament convention as soon as possible, which "Germany, regardless of its government, will faithfully fulfill." Chairman Henderson then stated that the decision to adjourn had been almost unanimously approved, and announced the adjournment of the General Committee. From then on, Chairman Henderson will preside over separate negotiations, which will begin tomorrow.

Davis Meets with Roosevelt 81

To Confer on US Policy Regarding Disarmament

Reuters, London, 29th: U.S. President Roosevelt's recalled representative to Europe, Davis, traveled to the Atlantic coast today to board the President's yacht and meet with Roosevelt to report on the situation of the Disarmament Conference, stating that European public opinion is gradually supporting disarmament, but the future depends on the stability of the German government. U.S. President Roosevelt believes that the reason the United States agreed to consult with Europe is entirely based on Europe's disarmament. Therefore, he instructed Davis to return to Europe within a week and redouble his efforts for peace and disarmament in accordance with his recent proposals.

Current State of the United States Navy 82

National News, San Pedro, 28th: After receiving the Navy Department's Fleet Relocation Procedure today, U.S. naval authorities here stated that virtually all naval aircraft and 161 warships will be stationed in the San Pedro and San Diego districts of the Pacific coast in the next fiscal year. The number of naval personnel will be maintained at 70 percent throughout the year, totaling 219 warships in service in various locations, with 54,150 officers and men. Some warships will be stationed at other bases on the Pacific coast, while others will be stationed on the Atlantic coast and at various overseas bases. The U.S. Naval Air Force has a total of 491 aircraft of various types and 3,498 officers and men. Also, according to Washington sources, the Navy Secretary has ordered that 800 workers, clerks, and technicians originally planned to be laid off from naval shipyards in various locations be placed on unpaid leave until September 30, as they are expected to be needed for the construction of new ships.

(Reuters, Vienna, 29th) The Austrian government is now prepared to adopt new sanction measures against the terrorist tactics employed by the National Socialist Party within Austria. Although the National Socialist Party's newspapers have been closed, they have now resumed publication, albeit in a slightly altered form. It is also reported that the Austrian authorities plan to expel all National Socialist Party spies who have stayed in Austria by changing their names or other methods.

Floodwaters in Wuhan Show No Sign of Retreating 100

Breach of the Hanyang Main Dike, Various Counties Report Danger

Provincial Government Submits Report on Flood Control to the Executive Yuan

(Correspondence from Hankou) The Yangtze River water in Wuhan has been rising for several days, and the trees on the Longhe Embankment are submerged in the vast expanse of water. Although it has not yet caused a major disaster, it is still alarming. The upstream water flow has now eased slightly, but Dongting and Poyang Lakes are overflowing simultaneously, and the river flow has nowhere to go, causing concerns about breaches in various embankments. Today, the 27th, according to a compilation of reports from various sources, there has been a collapse of the Xinhao Embankment in Hanyang, a breach of the Shuanghe Embankment, a collapse of Zhangjiadun, and seepage at Xintankou, Yongfeng Sluice Gate, Fuben Embankment, and Hama Isle. Xinhao Embankment is the county's largest civil embankment, bordering the Yangtze River to the east and the Dun River to the north, with approximately 17,000 mu of farmland within the embankment. Once it loses its protection, the losses are incalculable. In Wuchang, leakage has been discovered at the Zhoujiazui Sluice Gate downstream of Jinkou. In addition, the Hubei Lake Embankment is experiencing the simultaneous surge of the river and lake, posing extreme danger. Jizhiang is suffering from water accumulation and embankment alarms. The new embankment along the river is gradually collapsing, bringing the total to three breached embankments and seventeen dangerous ones. Wang, President of the Executive Yuan, is extremely concerned about the rising water in Hubei Province. On the 25th, he telegraphed Xia Douyin, Chairman of the Provincial Government, to inquire about the recent conditions of the embankments. Xia responded with an urgent telegram on the 26th, and formally submitted a report on the 27th, which reads as follows: "Report on reporting matters. I received a telegram from Your Excellency stating that according to reports, the river water has risen sharply, and instructing me to report on the embankment situation, etc. I am deeply grateful for Your Excellency's concern for the people's livelihood. Upon investigation, the Yangtze River and Han River areas experienced continuous heavy rains from late May to early June, and the water level has been increasing non-stop. This government is deeply concerned that the completion date for the embankment repairs undertaken by the Yangtze River and Han River Engineering Bureau has not yet been reported. We intended to implement temporary flood control measures and were about to announce them when we received an order from the General Headquarters for the Suppression of Bandits in the Henan, Hubei, and Anhui Provinces, issuing the 13 articles of the Yangtze River and Han River main embankment flood control measures drafted by the National Economic Commission, instructing us to comply immediately. After submitting the report to the Provincial Government Committee meeting, it was concluded that the flood control measures would shift the heavy responsibility of flood control to the local governments, with the Yangtze River and Han River Engineering Bureau only playing an assisting role, making it difficult to fully implement the measures. Therefore, we telegraphed Chiang Kai-shek in Nanchang, detailing that the province of Hubei depends on its embankments for its livelihood, the local vitality has not yet recovered, and the flood control funds and materials should be provided by the Yangtze River and Han River Engineering Bureau, and they should be responsible for handling all practical matters. At the same time, Li Fanyi, who is also the Director of the Construction Department, was publicly recommended to go to Nanchang to personally meet with Chiang Kai-shek to request instructions. Seeing that the rate of water increase exceeded the water level of the same month 20 years ago, we first announced the temporary flood control measures that this government had planned to prevent accidents. Subsequently, on June 11, we received a telegram from Chiang Kai-shek, instructing Li to work with Yang Silian, Director of the Yangtze River and Han River Engineering Bureau, to revise the measures and submit them for review. On June 15, we received another telegram from Chiang Kai-shek, instructing us to send personnel to attend the Five-Province Flood Prevention Committee jointly formed by the Yangtze River Waterway Commission, which was followed accordingly. On June 20, Li Fanyi, who is also the Director of the Construction Department, submitted the flood control measures and budget documents that he had negotiated and signed with the Director of the Yangtze River and Han River Engineering Bureau, and proposed the resolution of the 32nd Committee Meeting of this government, which was revised, passed, and circulated on June 21 for compliance. The county magistrates of the embankment counties were appointed as flood control committee members and flood prevention inspectors, assigned to various locations, and implemented the work. Fearing that the counties and cities would dispute material funds during flood control, overspend, falsely report in a panic, and delay in handling matters, five measures that must be followed during flood control were formulated and ordered to be followed by the Wuhan Municipal Government and the governments of 35 embankment counties. While preparing to submit the reports, we received the previous telegram. In addition to reporting the general situation in the previous telegram and reporting on future flood control matters one after another, we have compiled the relevant documents, stated the reasons and process, and submitted them for review and instructions. Furthermore, according to the Yangtze River and Han River Engineering Bureau's report on May 25, calculating the water level based on the Wu Song basic horizontal line, the water level in Wuchang was 22.03 meters. On June 24, it was 26.20 meters, an increase of 4.17 meters. The water level was relatively stable on the 25th and 26th. In Wuchang, the Construction Department has joined with various agencies to organize a temporary flood control committee for the provincial capital. In Hankou, the municipal government has also reported on the sectional flood control measures for the embankments along the river and the Zhanggong Embankment. As for the county embankments, the reported collapses are the Xinba of Jinkou, the Zhang Huinan Embankment of Shishou, and the Xinhao Embankment of Hanyang. A total of 17 embankments are reported to be in danger. I have compiled a list for submission and request your review." Furthermore, the Yangtze River and Han River Engineering Bureau was ordered to provide instructions on flood prevention measures, stating, "Upon investigation, after the General Headquarters issued the distribution of materials and funds to the government, we found that the funds and materials were too few and feared that they would be insufficient. We requested that the National Economic Commission be requested to quickly allocate the remaining 100,000 yuan of the original 200,000 yuan flood control funds requested by the bureau to meet the urgent needs. The bureau's allocation of funds and materials should be determined based on the length of the embankment, the degree of danger, and the transportation situation. For example, the Old Dragon Embankment is far away in Xiangyang and has been repeatedly reported to be in danger. The Jingjiang Embankment Engineering Bureau has jurisdiction over hundreds of miles of embankments, which are related to the livelihoods of more than ten counties, but only 2,000 yuan has been allocated, which is far too little. The Shuyang Engineering Office and the Shayang Engineering Office are full of dangerous projects, and the Second Engineering Office, which includes Wuhan, is also feared to have insufficient funds. Additional funds should be appropriately allocated when the second installment of funds is received. The distribution of materials and storage locations should be based on the convenience of transportation. In areas with difficult transportation and a lack of materials, more materials should be allocated. In areas with convenient transportation and easier purchases, more loans should be provided. Materials should also be pre-stored in suitable locations outside the locations of the various engineering offices as backup support for the engineering offices. The procedures for issuing funds and materials must be specified, and they must be prompt and practical, without any waste or abuse. In areas where wooden piles are not easily available, some wooden piles should also be prepared, or designated purchasing locations should be pre-assigned, in case of emergency. In short, this year's water level is too high and continues to rise, and future disasters are unpredictable. Flood control work is not only related to the livelihoods of a province and a county, but also to the entire national economy. Proper command and appropriate allocation will result in less cost and greater efficiency. Otherwise, even with a lot of money, there will be little real effect. I urge you to immediately cable the preparation office to allocate the original flood control funds in full and to quickly plan the most appropriate and convenient methods for allocating funds and materials in accordance with the above points to cope with the situation." (27th)

Japanese Armed Immigrants Build the False State of Jin 101

Manchurian Railway Supports Research Funding of 45,000 Yuan

False State Establishes Daxing Joint Stock Company

(Special Dispatch from Beiping) Recently, Japan plans to carry out large-scale immigration to the Northeast. The Manchurian Railway has designated a research fund of 45,000 yuan, with a term of two years. The research focuses on the food and nutritional components of the Northeast after the Japanese immigrants arrive, the digestion and absorption by the Japanese and their storage methods, how model houses in the Northeast should be transformed to suit Japanese living, and whether the clothes of the Northeast and Mongolia meet the physical requirements of the Japanese. Starting in June of this year, the Japanese Ministry of the Army began training a group of 500 immigrants in Gunma Prefecture, receiving military training for armed immigrants. At the same time, the Institute of Hygiene, in collaboration with the Manchurian Medical University, is conducting preliminary research on whether the clothing, food, and housing of the Northeast and Mongolia are suitable for Japanese immigrants. These immigration steps are solid evidence of the Japanese intention to permanently occupy the Northeast. In addition, the false organizations created by the Japanese have now established the Daxing Joint Stock Company, an affiliate of the Central Bank of Manchuria. The scale is very large, and its business includes seven types of operations: pawnshops, oil mills, distilleries, food, flour mills, papermaking, and forestry. The capital is set at 7 million yuan. The head office is located in Changchun, with branches in Fengtian, Jilin, Heilongjiang, and Qiqihar. Because the company is the valuation agency for agricultural products in the Manchurian state and the profit-making agency for large enterprises in Manchuria, it starts with food first. This system is exactly the same as the East India Company operated by the British in India. The Japanese goal is to start with commerce, absorb Manchurian capital, and develop Manchurian enterprises. Although the Daxing Joint Stock Company is of a national nature of the Manchurian state, the real boss behind the Manchurian state is Japan, which is no different from the Japanese operating it. This kind of commercial combination of economic systems can be transformed into a political organization, so the Daxing Joint Stock Company in the eyes of the Japanese is like the second East India Company, containing political properties. (27th)

Fang Zhenwu Issues Circular Telegrams for Several Days 102

(Correspondence from Beiping) Fang Zhenwu has repeatedly issued circular telegrams in Zhangjiakou for several days, making many proposals on the current situation. The following is a summary of the main points of each telegram: (1) Zhen Telegram opposes the cotton and wheat loan, stating that Song Ziwen, with the mission of the Nanjing government, borrowed 50 million US dollars from the American Finance Rehabilitation Corporation to buy cotton at 40% and wheat at 10%. Cotton and wheat are surplus goods in the United States. Moreover, in recent years, China's agricultural products have been oversupplied, grain prices have fallen, and when grains are cheap and hurt farmers, the economy will inevitably collapse. If a large amount of imported cotton and wheat are dumped again, it is tantamount to the capitalist countries absorbing the blood of our people and oppressing China's economy. Using this as a financial element is no different from drinking poison to quench thirst and hastening death. Zhenwu is untalented, a member of the Central Committee, driven by conscience, and for the sake of justice. He is determined to oppose Song Ziwen's cotton and wheat loan to the death. (2) Yuan Telegram advocates thorough resistance to Japan, stating that recently Japanese soldiers within the pass have continued to press on the border, and the situation in Eastern Chahar is tense again, which is heartbreaking. Hearing this makes one's hair stand on end. Zhenwu has stationed troops outside the border, determined to resist Japan, and is preparing for war without hesitation. As long as he has a breath left, he will swear to wield his armor and fight a mortal battle with the Japanese puppet troops, implementing the proposition of resisting Japan and saving the country, and will not make any compromises. He will seek justice for the country and fight for the survival of the nation, regardless of success or failure. (3) Shan Telegram states that China has vast land and abundant resources, and its culture and materials are unparalleled in the world. In the past, during the Qin Shi Huang, Han Wu Emperor, and Tang Taizong eras, their prestige reached everywhere, and all surrendered. But today, the country is fragmented, and families are displaced. This is due to the wicked Japanese chaebols, who have abandoned the affection of the same script and race and implemented their aggressive strategy. However, our country's authorities have failed to rise to the occasion, giving people an opportunity to take advantage. Zhenwu has been engaged in revolution for thirty years, with saving the country as a prerequisite and protecting the people as a priority. He vows to lead tens of thousands of troops, drive out the Japanese pirates, and return our territory, implementing the proposition of resisting Japan and saving the country. He will not stop fighting until the goal is achieved.

Guangcheng Embankment in Anhui Province Collapses 103

Many Other Embankments are Also in Danger

(Correspondence from Anqing) Recently, the Yangtze River water level has risen sharply. According to the water level in Anqing, it has now reached over 38 feet, and the situation is precarious. Anhui Province has suffered a severe flood in 1920, and the damage has not yet recovered. How can it withstand another disaster? The provincial government and the Civil Affairs and Construction Departments have ordered various counties to defend and sent personnel to supervise and guide. Liu Yiyan, Director of the Construction Department, recently personally inspected the embankments in the lower reaches of the Yangtze River, and Ma Lingfu, Director of the Civil Affairs Department, acting on behalf of the Chairman of the Provincial Government, also accompanied various provincial committee members to inspect the upper reaches on the 21st of the month and continued to inspect the lower reaches on the 24th and 25th, returning to the province on the morning of the 26th to attend the provincial government's extended memorial week and report the results of the inspection. The main points of Ma's report, combined with recent developments, are described as follows: (1) Ma Hua Embankment is related to the water conservancy of seven counties in Hubei, Jiangxi, and Anhui provinces, with a length of over a hundred miles in Anhui. Recently, the embankment body is still seven or eight feet above the water surface, and there may be no danger at present. The provincial government has sent two members from the Civil Affairs Department and one member from the Construction Department to investigate and protect it. (2) Baoxing Embankment is located east of Huayang Town in Wangjiang County. The embankment along the river is in good condition, but the transverse embankment is thin and cannot withstand wind and waves. The embankment directors should be ordered to quickly repair it. (3) Guangcheng Embankment is located upstream of Anqing, with over 800 zhang of sandy embankment along the river. There are many wave holes at the foot of the embankment, and the embankment surface has been eroded by water in many places, making it very dangerous. Ma ordered the Huaining County Magistrate to supervise the repair after returning to the province. Unfortunately, the embankment collapsed on the afternoon of the 26th during a storm and heavy rain, causing considerable damage. (4) Guangshu Embankment is located opposite Anqing, under the jurisdiction of Dongji County. The river embankment is currently about four feet above the water surface, and the embankment body is still solid. However, the eastern embankment and the Yangjia Yin area are very dangerous. Huang Yingzhong, a member of the Construction Department who accompanied Ma, was left at the embankment to conduct a detailed survey and supervise the county to handle it. (5) Guangji Embankment is related to the food supply of Huai and Tong counties. The current embankment surface is about five feet above the water, and firewood and grass bundles are being used to block the waves. However, a section near Majiawo has a sandy embankment and may not be able to withstand the wind and waves. The embankment committee should be ordered to gather manpower to strengthen protection and allocate funds to purchase emergency materials. (6) Chenjiazhou is located east of Guijia Dam in Tongcheng. The river embankment is still strong, and the embankment surface is about six feet above the water. However, the adjacent Xiadacheng Embankment and Zhijia Yin area are currently low and thin. Xiadacheng Embankment is 300 zhang long and only about two feet above the water. If the water surges in, it will affect dozens of miles. Shi Huacheng, a technician from the Construction Department, should be sent to conduct a detailed survey and also inspect the Guanzhuang Embankment in Tongling, the Baoda Embankment in Fanchang, the Xijiang Embankment along the Mabao Embankment in Wuhu, and the Daguan Embankment in Dangtu. (7) Datong Embankment is located east of Meigeng Town in Dongji. The lower section of the river embankment is not very strong, especially the Laoniu in the first embankment and the river embankment, which is only one or two feet above the water, are the most dangerous. The acting county magistrate should be telegraphed to pay special attention. (8) Guanzhuang Embankment is located in Tongling, also known as Renfeng Embankment. It has a large area, and both the river embankment and the inner embankment are very strong. The river embankment is about six feet above the water. However, the dam embankment head needs to be rebuilt. Shi Huacheng, a technician from the Construction Department, should be sent to conduct a survey. (9) Huangsitan is under the jurisdiction of Wuwei County and serves as a barrier for seven counties, including Hehan, Shulu, Chaohu, and Hehe, and is located on the Wei of the Yangtze River. It has been collapsing over the years, and the current embankment surface is only a little over four feet above the water. Moreover, the lower section is over 300 zhang long and is only two feet above the water, requiring urgent protection. Zhang Bochang, a member of the Civil Affairs Department, and Wang Deyu, a technician from the Construction Department, should be ordered to station at the embankment to guide protection and conduct detailed surveys upstream and downstream. (June 28)

Frequent Alarms Regarding the North Lu Canal 104

The Construction Department Dispatches Personnel to Various Counties to Supervise and Expedite Emergency Reinforcements

Jinan dispatch: The water level in the North Lu Canal (i.e., the Wei River) rose sharply the day before yesterday, reaching 29 meters, very close to the danger line. Eleven dangerous spots have been discovered along the river near Yanzhuang, and alarms are frequently being raised. Upon receiving the report, Zhang Honglie, the head of the Construction Department, considering that the North Lu area has suffered from frequent floods in recent years, and the water level is rising so steeply even before the summer flood season, urgently ordered the intensification of emergency reinforcements to prevent accidents. He specifically dispatched technical assistants Qu Changqian to Guantao, Sun Weihan to Linqing, Yu Zhuntai to Xiajin, technician Sun Ziyun to Wucheng, Yao Xintian to De County, and committee member Zuo Shaoji to En County to supervise and expedite the emergency reinforcements. In addition to informing the county magistrates of the six counties by telegram, he ordered the technical assistants and technicians to depart immediately and formulated eight measures, ordering the technical assistants and technicians to inspect the river works conditions for any dangerous sections upon arriving in each county, together with the county magistrate, the head of the Fourth Section, and the district chiefs. They are to set up water level gauges and record the water level fluctuations, mutually informing neighboring counties by telephone for prevention. The necessary labor and materials are to be the responsibility of the affected districts. In addition, a telegram was sent to Wucheng County Magistrate Zhen Guangyuan to forward to Sun Ziyun, approving the temporary use of funds needed for the dangerous sections in Yanzhuang, to be reimbursed by the county magistrate later, to meet urgent needs. The arrangements were extremely thorough, and the river works may be free from danger. Furthermore, technician Yao Xintian is currently supervising the construction of a sand embankment in En County and Wucheng (the two counties previously engaged in armed clashes due to embankment construction). In a few more days, the embankment construction can be completed. If the sand embankment is successful, the flood disasters in En and Wucheng counties can be reduced. The following are the eight measures from the Construction Department's instructions assigning special commissioners to be stationed in various counties along the river to supervise and guide emergency reinforcement:

(1) After the committee member arrives at the county, he shall immediately convene a meeting with the county magistrate, the head of the Fourth Section, and the district chiefs along the river to discuss emergency reinforcement measures, organization, and procedures, and submit them to the department for record. (2) After the committee member arrives at the county, he must inspect along the river for one week together with the head of the Fourth Section. If there are dangerous sections, he should immediately notify the county magistrate to implement emergency reinforcement measures quickly according to regulations. (3) The labor and materials used for emergency reinforcement should be the responsibility of the affected districts to raise. (4) The Fourth Section of the county government should select a suitable location to install a water level gauge and assign a dedicated person to record the water level regularly. (The location for installing the gauge should be near a telephone, and if one has already been set up, it can be omitted.) (5) The personnel recording the water level should also report the water level fluctuations at any time, first by telephone to the committee member of this department, who will transmit it to the committee members of neighboring counties, and also report to the county government, and then fill out a form to submit to the county government for record. (6) The recording time is three times a day, at 7:00 am, 12:00 pm, and 5:00 pm, but in special circumstances, it must be recorded at any time. (7) The committee member's residence should be near the water gauge location or the district office. (8) The committee member must report the water level fluctuations, fill in the form, and report to the department every three days.

Charcoal-Powered Vehicle Engine Factory Established in Hankou 105

Hankou dispatch: Since the advent of automobiles, China has not been able to manufacture them ourselves, and the sales of gasoline have been enormous, resulting in an astonishing outflow of funds every year. Since the opening of highways in various provinces, the loss is even greater where public buses operate.

Tang Zhongming's charcoal-powered vehicle engine to replace gasoline engines has long been publicized. Mr. Tang studied in France for many years and devoted himself to the automotive industry. After returning to China, he researched and manufactured charcoal-powered vehicle engines for five years, using charcoal instead of gasoline. First, the fuel is very cheap and readily available everywhere; second, driving can be entirely supplied by domestic products, which will greatly benefit the national economy. Trial results in various provinces of Henan, Shanxi, and the capital have been deemed stable and applicable. All newspapers have reported on this. It is understood that the charcoal-powered vehicle engine was originally invented by the French, but the research was not perfect and was declared a failure. The machines made by the French could not travel long distances, were slower than gasoline, could not climb steep slopes, and were bulky. The machines manufactured by Mr. Tang can avoid the above disadvantages, so everyone is generally satisfied. Yan Xishan, the Pacification Commissioner of Shanxi-Suiyuan, and Xiong Shihui, the chairman of Jiangxi Province, heard that this charcoal-powered engine was beneficial to the people's livelihood and invited him to set up factories in their respective provinces, but it did not materialize due to various reasons. Recently, Mr. Li Hesheng of Hankou invited Mr. Tang to cooperate, hired him as the chief engineer, and established a factory to manufacture them themselves, named the China Coal Gas Engine Manufacturing Factory, located on Shenchang Street. This reporter was invited to visit. The factory occupies a large area, and after a short period of operation, the scale is roughly complete. Goods have already been shipped to Shaanxi, Henan, and Sichuan provinces. The Beijing and Hankou municipal governments have also purchased and applied them. Even the American Dodge Motor Company has purchased many units and installed them on new cars to attract customers.

The factory's output currently cannot meet demand. After the equipment is expanded, it is being added one after another. If the equipment is expanded, the daily output will be more than 100 engines. According to the factory, this charcoal engine is most suitable for long-distance buses because the charcoal material is most abundant in the interior. After starting, there is no short-distance stop. As for the form of the engine body, the initial model was very large and lacked beauty. It has now been improved to create a refined style. Those installed on ordinary vehicles are covered with boxes to hide them, without revealing their shape, and do not damage the original appearance.

The factory provides on-site installation for local customers who purchase the engine and ships them in boxes to distant customers, sending personnel to handle them and provide instructions on how to use them. A training class has now been established in the factory to recruit junior and senior high school graduates, provide them with practical training and lectures, and graduate them in the shortest time. In the future, they will be sent to various places to serve. The factory has obtained patent rights from the Ministry of Industry. Mr. Li is now paying attention to the northwestern provinces, and in the future, he plans to promote it in the southeastern provinces. There are currently more than 300 workers in the factory, and the treatment is quite comprehensive. In addition to the training class, accommodation is also provided. The factory and dormitory are clean. A large-scale dormitory is being renovated, which can accommodate at least several hundred people. The factory has a wide area, fine grass like a carpet, green shade everywhere, and fresh air. If it can maintain its reputation and strive for perfection in the future, it will not be difficult to expand its scope.

After Huo Weizhou Was Assassinated 106

Yang Chongren, Principal of Min Tuo Middle School

Confesses He Was Ordered to Kill Huo

The Circumstances of the Memorial Service Held by Fellow Townsmen from the Northeast 107

A dispatch from Peiping: After Huo Weizhou, a committee member of the Northeast People's Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association, was assassinated, his coffin was placed in Fayuan Temple. Northeast dignitaries Bao Yulin, Wang Huayi, Wang Zhuoran, and others, remembering Huo's sacrifice for the country, held a memorial service at Fayuan Temple yesterday (the 25th). More than 300 people from all walks of life attended the memorial service. Wang Zhuoran presided over the meeting, and Gao Chongmin reported on Huo's life and deeds. Details are recorded below:

Arrangement of the Funeral Hall 108

The funeral hall was set up in the east wing of the rear of Fayuan Temple. A portrait of Huo was hung in the center. Three plain colored arches were erected in front of the hall, adorned with the words "Sacrificed for the Country." More than 220 elegiac couplets and more than 40 floral wreaths were hung inside and outside the courtyard and the funeral hall. In addition, Zhu Qinglan sent a horizontal plaque inscribed with "Eternal Ambition." Huo's family members were all behind the funeral hall, covered in white cloth, and the tragic cries were endless, which was particularly heartbreaking. Guests were divided between the southwest and northwest wings. Inside and outside the temple, Yuan Hualun, the director of the Fourth District Police Department, led patrol officers to maintain order.

The Situation of the Public Memorial Service 109

The meeting began at 2:00 PM, and the ceremony was performed as required. Wang Zhuoran, a committee member of the Northeast People's Anti-Japanese Association, presided over the ceremony and offered a floral wreath. Gao Chongmin reported on Huo's life and deeds and the circumstances of the assassination. After Gao's report, Yang Daguang, a guest, gave a speech, followed by Zhou Chongxun, Huo's cousin, who gave a reply. Finally, Ms. Xiang Shouzhen, Huo's wife, thanked the attendees. Then, photos were taken and the meeting adjourned.

Huo's Aftermath 110

Huo was extremely honest and had no savings. This sudden assassination left his family in dire straits. In addition to the 1,000 yuan allocated by Zhu Qinglan, the funeral expenses were borne by Huo's relatives and friends. The coffin will be temporarily placed in Fayuan Temple, and after the lost territories of the East Province are recovered, it will be moved to Huo's original burial place in Kaiyuan County, Liaoning. Currently, the living problems are being actively addressed by relatives and friends. Huo's daughter, Wenying, is sixteen years old and will be chosen by relatives and friends to marry. Huo's eldest son is planned to be sent to a school to study, and the remaining three sons are still young and will be raised to adulthood to carry on their father's legacy.

Memorial Oration at the Assembly 111

"On the twenty-fifth day of June in the twenty-second year of the Republic of China, Wang Zhuoran and others respectfully offer clear wine and sacrifices to the spirit of Mr. Huo, saying: Alas, Mr. Huo, with innate brilliance and outstanding talent, you quickly gained fame. At a young age, you carried your books to the gates of Yan, delved into scholarship, and achieved profound attainments. After completing your studies, you taught in your hometown, patiently guiding and tirelessly speaking. The fate of the nation was at its lowest, the political program collapsed, and powerful neighbors surrounded us, recklessly invading. You were deeply concerned about the state of affairs and were determined to save the country and turn weakness into strength. You put your words into action, stood firm in your ambition, mobilized the people, and united them. During the Shenyang Incident, you rushed to the old capital to participate in the resistance against Japan and seek recovery. For two years, you were spirited and energetic, not avoiding difficulties and dangers, and exhausting your wisdom. You hoped that your talents could be used to drive out the Japanese invaders and express the pain of the lost province. But on a thoroughfare, a sudden and violent assailant came, and you died with your ambition. Alas, how painful! I think of your demeanor, generous and tolerant, shining like the sun and moon, and gentle like the spring breeze. You were intelligent and sharp, with extraordinary courage, firm in your beliefs, and distinguished from the crowd. You deeply despised peace and contention, abandoning profit and embracing righteousness. Everyone wanted to seize power, but you only made clear your ambition. Heaven did not pity us and took away our wise man. Our homeland is lost, and the building is about to collapse. Your great ambition was not realized, and your coffin is a thousand miles away. Your wife is a widow, and your children are young, weeping with tears. Alas, Weizhou, your form has passed, but your spirit remains. You lived as a righteous man and died as a hero. We, your friends, grieve for you with deep sorrow. We are eternally separated by life and death, and our sadness is endless. We set up sacrifices and pour a glass of wine. May your soul be present and enjoy our offerings. Alas, woe!"

The Main Culprit is Arrested 112

After Huo Weizhou was assassinated and killed in Peiping, the Second District Police Department successively arrested more than ten people, including Yang Chongren, the principal of Min Tuo Middle School, at the Litong Hotel in Dongjiaomin Lane, and took them to the Second District Police Department for interrogation. After separate investigations by Yin Huanran, the head of the district police department, Yang and others initially admitted that they were members of the National Socialist Party and that Min Tuo Middle School was the operating agency of the National Socialist Party in Peiping, but they did not admit that they were involved in the assassination of Huo. Later, after the police department presented witnesses Shao (Yang's friend) and Wang Wentao, also known as Wang Zizhen (a female teacher at the school), as evidence, Yang admitted that Huo Weizhou was an important member of the National Socialist Party, but now he had betrayed the party, which had a major impact on the party, so he was ordered by the party to kill Huo, and he sent someone to assassinate him. Since there is a main culprit in this case, it is not necessary to pursue who the murderer is. The other suspects also gave the same confession as Yang, and they were all silent about the murderer. Therefore, the district police department hired three cars on the night of the 23rd and sent more than ten suspects in the case to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation. It was also learned that Yang had made considerable arrangements before sending someone to kill Huo, planning to flee to the Litong Hotel in Dongjiaomin Lane immediately after the assassination, and then be introduced by the wife of his friend Shao (who is French) to another French person, who would ensure his escape from Peiping. However, when Shao designed to hide him in the Litong Hotel after Huo was assassinated and Yang came to the hotel to meet him, he went to the Second District Police Department to inform on him. The police department dispatched plainclothes detectives to arrest Yang and the other suspects. The shocking case was finally solved. According to reliable sources this morning (the 26th), Shao in the Huo case is not his real name. He once studied diplomacy in France and once served as the secretary of the deputy commander-in-chief before Zhang Liang went abroad. His wife is quite famous in the social circles of Peiping and has frequent contact with ministers of various countries. He has been living in a certain place in the east of the city and has now been released on bail, it is said. (26th)

Local News

The Yangtze River Shipping Industry is Declining 120

Various Companies Suspend Services and Reduce Sailings

Since the January 28th Incident, business in the Yangtze River shipping industry has been increasingly sluggish. Recently, since the Yangtze River has been in flood, both upstream and downstream imports and exports have been in short supply, resulting in fewer goods and more ships, and an excess of tonnage. In order to maintain long-term operations, various shipping companies in this port have proposed reducing services and tightening operations. The details are recorded below:

Failure to Maintain Freight Rates 121

Currently, the Yangtze River route is operated by Taikoo, Jardine Matheson, China Merchants, Sanbei, NingShao, Jiejiang, Xiangtai, Nisshin, Minsheng, and other shipping companies. Taikoo, Jardine Matheson, China Merchants, and Sanbei all have regular scheduled services, but there are also many unscheduled "wild chicken" services. Recently, the major companies, in view of the excessive competition and price cutting of Yangtze River freight, which has caused significant losses in revenue, agreed that downstream goods should be charged at a fixed rate with a double nine discount plus a 1.95 commission, and no further price drops would be allowed. This measure was tried for two weeks, but it failed. Customers in Hankou did not ship large quantities of goods.

Sharp Decline in Imports and Exports 122

The shortage of goods on Yangtze River ships this year is rare in recent years. The main reason is that the people's purchasing power is weak, resulting in a sharp drop in goods going from Shanghai, which is only about two-sevenths of what it was before the January 28th Incident. The situation is the same for both incoming and outgoing goods, and the same is true for Taikoo, Jardine Matheson, China Merchants, Sanbei, NingShao, and other ships. In normal times, Taikoo and Jardine Matheson could receive up to 10,000 yuan in freight for each Yangtze River ship when there were many goods for export, and at least 15,000 to 16,000 yuan for a round trip. But now, the freight income for a single voyage is less than 5,000 yuan, while the expenses, including fuel, are at least 6,000 yuan.

No Remedial Measures Yet 123

Various shipping companies have suffered huge losses in business on the Yangtze River route and cannot reduce the expenses of each ship. Therefore, the major companies held a special meeting last Saturday to discuss remedial measures. They concluded that the people were impoverished, finances were exhausted, and there was a shortage of cargo transportation, so there was really no way to remedy the business. As a result, no measures were agreed upon.

Suspension of Services and Reduction of Sailings Implemented 124

Currently, the four companies of Taikoo, Jardine Matheson, China Merchants, and Sanbei have more than 40 Yangtze River ships, plus Nisshin, Xiangtai, Jiejiang, and others, resulting in an excess of tonnage. In order to reduce losses, each company has formulated passive maintenance methods and is implementing the suspension of services for Yangtze River ships that are older and consume more fuel. All companies will implement this uniformly, and Jardine Matheson has decided to suspend the operation of the Lianhe service starting from July 3.

The Bankers Association Held its Annual Meeting Yesterday 125

Chairman Li Fuxun Reported on the Association's Activities

The Bankers Association held its fourth annual meeting at 4:30 PM yesterday at the Association’s auditorium, No. 4 Hong Kong Road.

Representatives from the Bank of China, Bank of Communications, National Industrial Bank of China, Zhejiang Industrial Bank, Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank, Salt Industry Bank, Chung Fu Bank, Sze Ming Commercial Bank, China Banking Corporation, Guangdong Provincial Bank, Kin Cheng Banking Corporation, The New China Trust and Savings Bank, Tung Lai Bank, The Continental Bank, The Bank of East Asia, Wing Hang Bank, The Chinese Guanye Bank, China General Chamber of Commerce Bank, Bank of Communications of Southern China, Overseas Chinese Bank, Jiangsu Bank, The China State Bank, Ken Yieh Bank, Chung Hing Bank, The Farmers Bank of China, The National Goods Bank, Tung Woo Bank, National Commercial Bank, The Hongkong and Shanghai Banking Corporation, and other banks, including Xu Ji, Qian Xin-zhi, Xu Xin-liu, and Li Fuxun, a total of sixty-seven people attended. Secretary-General Lin Kanghou was also present.

The Chairman reported that the total number of bank representatives was one hundred and twenty-eight, of which sixty-seven were present, sufficient to meet the legal quorum. He then rang the bell to commence the meeting. Chairman Li Fuxun reported on the association's activities, stating that the association was about to enter its second year since its establishment. Important matters handled in the past had been reported at each general membership meeting. Now that the fourth general meeting was at hand, he had reviewed the case files from the past half-year and selected several important matters that could be reported to all members. He presented a summary for consideration by the members. (1) Abolishing the Tael and Adopting the Yuan: The most significant matter for the financial community this year was the abolition of the tael and adoption of the yuan. The motivation to promote the abolition of the tael in the banking industry dates back more than a decade. It had been brewed over repeatedly but was difficult to achieve. This year, the government resolved to reform the currency system and announced a fixed conversion rate between silver dollars and taels in February. Shortly thereafter, the Ministry of Finance resolutely ordered the implementation of the abolition of the tael on April 5. The association immediately convened an emergency joint meeting of silver and money industries that evening. In order to assist the government in promoting good governance, the banks and money shops were the first to unanimously comply. However, in haste, there were many complex details that needed to be planned perfectly to avoid obstacles. Therefore, meetings were held day and night, and telegrams and letters were exchanged frequently. A forward bill registration office was established within a short period of time. After a period of ten days, things gradually progressed. Other industries and foreign banks that were still waiting and watching also successively implemented the policy. The historical anomalous currency system was thus eliminated in one fell swoop, which was not only a fortunate event for the financial community but also a successful initial step for the future of monetary policy. (2) Petitioning the Ministry of Finance to Formulate Regulations for Minting Decimal Silver Subsidiary Coins: After the implementation of the abolition of the tael, unifying silver subsidiary coins was also an urgent task. China's currency system has always been complex and indescribable. Shanghai, where people from all walks of life gather, is especially full of light silver coins and copper coins. They are difficult to use and have a significant impact on the livelihoods of ordinary people. The Ministry of Finance, aware of this, solicited the opinions of the association. After research by a subcommittee, both palliative and fundamental solutions were drafted and submitted to the Ministry of Finance, instructing customs offices to strictly prohibit imports while also expediting the formulation of decimal silver subsidiary coin minting regulations to promote the unification of the currency system. The Ministry of Finance is currently coordinating and organizing the matter, and implementation is expected soon. (3) Establishment of a Rural Financial Adjustment Committee: Rural areas have been declining year by year, which is enough to shake the foundations of the country. In May of this year, the Executive Yuan organized the Rural Reconstruction Committee to seek ways to provide relief. At the same time, it sent a letter to the association, ordering it to organize a Rural Financial Adjustment Committee to assist in the effort. The association nominated twenty-one people, including Zhang Gongquan, to form the committee. However, due to the importance of the matter, empty words were insufficient. A definitive plan was necessary, and the government needed to make substantial efforts to advocate for rural relief. Therefore, the committee is currently still under consultation. (4) Pledging Donations for Airplanes and Relief for Northeastern Refugees: In March of this year, when the Rehe War was in crisis, people across the country felt deep sorrow and indignation. For a time, there was a surge in contributions to support the army. The association, not wanting to be left behind in patriotism, also launched a salary donation campaign among its employees, hoping to provide a small contribution to the military. However, the war situation was unfavorable, and the morale of the people declined as a result, and the matter was interrupted. Later, the Shanghai Municipal Government and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce sought donations for airplanes, and Zhu Ziqiao and Xiong Jiansan, seeing the plight of the displaced Northeastern refugees, also went out to raise funds. The association believed that the airplane donation was related to national defense, and it could not bear to stand idly by while the refugees were suffering. Therefore, the executive committee decided to have each bank pledge donations based on the previously reported salary donation amounts from their employees. A total of more than 45,800 yuan was raised. In May, the funds were distributed, with 10,000 yuan for the purchase of airplanes by the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, 15,000 yuan for the purchase of airplanes by the Municipal Government, and more than 20,800 yuan to Zhu Ziqiao and Xiong Bing-san for relief for Northeastern refugees. Official receipts were obtained for each transaction. This was the duty of each bank to the country and society, and the association was only acting as an agent to facilitate the matter. (Omitted remaining text)

Passed Resolutions: (1) Approved the budget of the previous term and the upcoming term for this year. (2) Approved the change of name of the Ho Feng Bank to the Overseas Chinese Bank and requested correction of the record. (3) Approved the replacement of member representatives from Zhejiang Industrial Bank, Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank, The Continental Bank, Guangdong Provincial Bank, China Banking Corporation, Tung Lai Bank, Overseas Chinese Bank, Hongkong and Shanghai Banking Corporation, and National Commercial Bank. (4) Approved the addition of member representatives from China General Chamber of Commerce Bank. The meeting adjourned at approximately 5:00 PM.

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Promotes Chinese Insurance 126

And Requests Setting Limits on Foreign Merchant Notaries

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce's Fourth Representative Assembly resolved to petition the Ministry of Industry to set limits on the ability of foreign merchants to act as notaries. At the same time, it notified all members not to purchase fire insurance from foreign merchant companies. The petition and notification are detailed below.

Petition to the Ministry of Industry 127

Regarding the petition: The Chamber convened its Fourth Representative Assembly on the 25th of this month to discuss the proposal put forward by Executive Committee Member Ma Shaoquan and others, stating, "It has been found that the fire insurance industry originated with the British and then spread to Europe and the United States. It has been practiced in our country for several decades. Its main purpose is to prepare for the unexpected and ensure safety, which is an excellent principle. However, in the event of a claim, disputes often arise between the insurer and the insured regarding compensation. In order to find a fair and impartial way to resolve these disputes, it is necessary to involve a third party to mediate. This third party is the fire insurance notary. Therefore, the notary's position embodies the nature of arbitration and exercises the function of appraisal, which is extremely important to the interests of both parties and their legal standing. In European and American countries, those engaged in the business of notary public must first register with the government and obtain permission before they can practice. However, foreign merchant notaries are now established throughout our country. They have not registered with our government or obtained permission from the local authorities. They are established freely and without any restrictions. This not only violates international practice but also infringes upon our legal rights. At a time when political tutelage is just beginning and legal rights are being sought to be recovered, our government is gradually restricting foreign lawyers, accountants, and others, but it allows these notaries to encroach upon our rights. They exercise their power throughout the country. Regardless of whether their arguments are fair or not, they disgrace our national prestige more than anything else. This is still the infringement of rights by foreign merchant insurance companies entrusting foreign merchant notaries. Recently, when Chinese insurance companies encounter claims, they also hire foreign merchant notaries to handle the assessment. The insurance company is established by Chinese, and the insured are also Chinese. Yet, foreigners are used as notaries to make assessments, which is even more absurd. Moreover, foreign merchant notaries use foreign languages with incomprehensible wording, deliberately distorting the facts. Even if there are disputes, they often dismiss them on the grounds that they are not valid. There are still cases that have been pending for several years, further proving the deep pain suffered by the Chinese people. The various chambers of commerce in the ports have appealed for assistance because of the oppression of foreign merchant notaries. Therefore, we hereby present the following remedies: (1) Notify all trade associations and inform the chambers of commerce in various places to inform their respective members that they should promote Chinese insurance businesses in the future. If a foreign merchant notary is used by the insurance company when a claim occurs, it should be rejected. (2) Send a special letter to the Shanghai Chinese Insurance Association, asking it to instruct its member companies not to use foreign merchant notaries again in order to uphold national prestige. (3) Petition the government to strictly crack down on foreign merchant notaries abusing the powers of a notary public and request that a public decision be made." The motion was passed. The first item was notified to all trades for compliance, and the second and third items were submitted separately for review and approval. Limiting foreign merchant notaries from exercising their powers requires the government to clearly define laws and regulations, implement registration procedures, and establish the principle that Chinese merchants should serve as notaries. It is difficult to reverse the accumulated trend. The association, based on the resolutions of the Second General Assembly in the 20th year of the Republic of China, petitioned for review and approval but did not receive a response. Now, based on the foregoing, we hereby re-submit the case and petition Your Ministry to review, approve, and promptly define measures and notify all subordinates to comply with them, which would be for the public good.

Notice to All Trades 128

Respectfully, on the 25th of this month, the Chamber convened its Fourth Representative Assembly to discuss the proposal of Supervisor Fang Jiaobo, which stated, in brief, "The insurance industry is of great importance to the national economy and the interests of the insured. Please submit to the General Assembly for a resolution to notify all trades and commercial organizations to inform their respective members that all group or private property that is to be insured should be insured with Chinese insurance companies. This will not only prevent the leakage of money but also avoid the dangers when a claim occurs. Is this appropriate? Please vote on it." The motion was passed, and all trade associations were notified to comply with it. In addition to sending separate letters, we hereby notify you. Please inform your fellow merchants to comply. Otherwise, if disputes arise in the future due to insurance with foreign merchant companies and assistance is requested, it should not be accepted. This is of utmost importance.

According to the Guowen News Agency, a mutiny broke out in the Qingdao Navy to overthrow Shen Honglie.
