Sailing to Miao Island 130

According to sources, the cruisers Haiqi and Haichen, the training cruiser Zhaoh and the gunboats Zhenhai and Chuyu from the Qingdao Navy have sailed away from Qingdao and are currently at Miao Island (outside the port of Penglai County). However, Miao Island is barren. The reason for sailing there is unknown. Although it is said that the captains of the five warships have landed, it seems that the initiative was taken by lower-ranking officers. It is unlikely that the entire group landed. There must be one or two captains involved in the joint action. If this was an action by soldiers, then the warships could not have sailed if even the lower-ranking officers had landed.

Factional Strife 131

As for the Qingdao Navy, it broke away from the Northeast Fleet. Recently, there have been relatively few people from Fujian and Guangdong, and those from Shandong have also been eliminated. Most are from the Hubei and Jiangsu-Zhejiang factions. Talk of surrendering to the puppet regime is an overreaction. Most of the officers are from Hubei, Shandong, Jiangsu, and Zhejiang provinces. It would be even more difficult to go to Guangdong because the central navy is blocking the way, and there is a shortage of coal and water. It is difficult to travel long distances without stopping.

Chu Minyi Discusses the Current Situation 134

600,000 Yuan has been Allocated for Flood Control

The Central Government Pays Attention to Flood Prevention Work 135

According to Chu, the Central Government attaches great importance to flood prevention work and has instructed the Ministry of Finance to allocate 600,000 yuan for flood prevention, which is needed for protecting long dikes and other projects. The Yangtze River Waterways Board is the central agency for flood prevention. The chairman of the board, Zhou Xiangxian, has already flown to Jiujiang and will be stationed in Xunyang to oversee flood prevention work both upstream and downstream. The Executive Yuan has also instructed the authorities in various provinces to strictly prevent floods. In addition to the provinces raising funds on their own, the Central Government will provide appropriate subsidies. August is the season with the highest water levels each year. The river water in June this year has been particularly high, exceeding the water level in mid-June of the 20th year of the Republic of China by several feet. If the dredging is smooth, the river water is expected to rise again in mid-August, but it is hoped that it will not cause a disaster.

Turmoil in the Northeast Fleet 136

The Mayor of Qingdao and Commander of the Northeast Fleet, Shen Honglie, was assassinated and frightened. The Central Government sent a telegram to express its condolences. The five warships Haiqi, Haichen, and Zhaoh left Qingdao because they opposed Shen. It was purely a personal matter. The rumors that they would defect to the puppet regime are not accurate. The Central Government has not yet received a detailed report on the turmoil, nor has it received Shen's resignation. The newspaper reports that Shen has telegraphed the Central Government to resign from all his positions are not accurate. The Central Government must wait until it receives a detailed report before handling the matter. It is hoped that the situation will not escalate.

Water Levels are Receding Rapidly Upstream

During the great flood of the 20th year of the Republic of China, the old dikes on both sides of the Yangtze and Han rivers collapsed when the water was 45 feet high. Now, the water level is two feet and two inches higher than in the previous year, and the dikes are still intact, which is enough to prove that the dikes built last year are solid. All necessary flood control work is being handled by the Jianghan Engineering Department of the council. The recruitment of laborers in case of emergency has been properly negotiated and regulated with the provincial government and local authorities. All materials for engineering applications have also been prepared in advance and transported to appropriate locations for use in case of dike emergencies. The dangerous period has now passed. Hankou has had several days of sunny weather last week, and the water level has been 47.2 feet. The height of the upstream stations has also been dropping repeatedly, indicating that the river water has stabilized and will not continue to surge. The bandit forces in Jiangxi are collapsing, and the National Army is in pursuit.

Taking Advantage of the Victory to Pursue and Suppress: The bandit trouble in Jiangxi Province persists. The besieging army has taken advantage of the victory to advance and suppress, aiming to directly attack the bandit nests and resolve the people's difficulties.

Time Limit for Clearing Out Red Bandits in Jiangxi Province: According to the latest investigation, although it is difficult to obtain an accurate number, there are likely around 70,000 firearms. The National Army for bandit suppression numbers over 200,000. He Jian in the west, Chen Jitang in the south, and Liu Zhenhua, etc., will jointly encircle and suppress. Therefore, within three months, although it may not be possible to completely eliminate the Jiangxi bandits, it will certainly not be difficult to destroy their main forces. The National Army for bandit suppression does not have exclusive authority over bandit suppression; expenses are allocated according to the original military budget. Rumors of raising bandit suppression public bonds are not true, he said.

Difficulties in Bandit Suppression: Bandit suppression work is extremely difficult, because there are often good and innocent people implicated among the bandits. While suppressing the bandits, the Central Army must also appease the good people. This kind of war can be called a war for the people. It is necessary to make the masses repent and awaken. Therefore, the suppression also involves persuasion work, which is more difficult than any other war.

Responsible for Relief: As for the bandit areas that have already been recovered, the central and local governments are responsible for relief, striving for the revival of the rural areas. The villagers in these areas have suffered robbery and slaughter by the Red bandits. Without substantial relief, the people will not be able to live and work in peace. The central government has already formulated measures for relieving the recovered bandit areas, such as building bandit-proof projects to prevent the bandits from invading again, and recruiting vagrants and local bullies to avoid their being used by the bandits. All of these have been handled according to the set measures. As for the internal organization of the communists, whether male or female, young or old, they all have considerable organization, so the severity of the damage to the local area is indeed beyond what we can achieve.

Chahar Situation: Mr. Yang also said that Chairman Chiang has always maintained a peaceful attitude towards the Chahar incident, hoping to resolve it peacefully within the possible scope. He also hopes that Feng Huanzhang will leave Chahar as soon as possible. Mr. Feng has no real power; what he relies on is the anti-Japanese banner. Mr. Ge Baichuan has always taken the central government's intention as his intention and has no problems. It was recently learned that Central Committee member Kong Xiangxi will go north to mediate the Chahar affairs, but it is now said that this trip may be canceled. Mr. Yang plans to stay in Shanghai for a few days before going to Nanjing to report. Mr. Yang has denied rumors that he will preside over Hubei province.

Mr. William Martin, editor of the Geneva newspaper, arrived in Shanghai by night train from Nanjing the night before last. New Tax Rates for Liquor and Tobacco to Take Effect Tomorrow 155

Ministry of Finance Orders Seven Provincial Bureaus to Comply

And Promulgate to the People in Various Places for General Knowledge

In order to rectify the liquor and tobacco tax, the Ministry of Finance plans to abolish the public sales system and separately formulate regulations on special taxes for native tobacco leaves and fixed tax rates for native liquor. It is scheduled to begin on July 1st, with pilot implementation in the seven provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Henan, Hubei, Jiangxi, and Fujian. Although the Shanghai-Nanjing-Suzhou Tobacco and Liquor Trade Association went to Beijing to petition, it was ultimately not accepted. Therefore, the new tax rates are inevitable. It is learned that the Ministry of Finance yesterday issued an order to the stamp tax bureaus for tobacco and liquor in the seven provinces, limiting the collection to begin on July 1st, and to promulgate it widely for general knowledge.

General Order 156

Regarding the implementation of orders, the fixed tax for native liquor in the seven provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Henan, Hubei, Jiangxi, and Fujian is scheduled to begin on July 1st of this year. The Taxation Department has already issued orders to the bureaus in each province to comply, and has successively issued regulations and sample documents. However, at the beginning of implementing a new system, it is necessary to clearly inform the merchants and people of the purpose of the reform to avoid misunderstandings. Therefore, the Ministry has drafted a proclamation, which is issued to the bureaus in each province to forward to their respective sub-bureaus for widespread posting, so that even remote rural areas may be informed. The main points of the regulations on the collection of fixed tax and the fixed tax rates for native liquor should also be announced in detail by the bureaus in each province so that merchants can comply. This fixed tax must be initiated on July 1st of this year as scheduled. All previously collected public sales fees and taxes will be canceled from the same date and no longer collected. The existing local surtaxes should continue to be handled temporarily according to the previous number and limit of the old cases. If there are no surtax items, no new ones should be added. In addition to instructing the stamp tax bureaus for tobacco and liquor in each province to comply, and consulting the governments of each province to instruct local officials to assist in the implementation, this order is issued with a copy of the proclamation and draft consultation, ordering the bureaus to comply. Furthermore, this reform is the initial foundation for establishing unified collection. The bureau chiefs must supervise their subordinates to faithfully implement it. If there is any insincere compliance, it will be severely punished upon discovery, without any leniency. This is of utmost importance. This order.

Proclamation 157

Regarding the matter of the Proclamation, the method of taxation values simplicity, and the key to reform lies in uniformity. The current tax system for native tobacco and liquor in various provinces has long followed old customs. The provinces are extremely diverse, and the procedures are inconsistent. Each province governs itself, and the rules are difficult to follow. Deep-seated malpractices have caused difficulties for both superiors and subordinates. Unless it is cleared up on a large scale, it will not be sufficient to enrich taxes and benefit the people. The Ministry has considered the situation, deliberated several times, and believes that the way to improve is to simplify and unify the collection. In March of this year, the Taxation Department was ordered to convene a meeting of the directors of the stamp tax bureaus for tobacco and liquor in each province to determine principles and begin rectification. Now, the tax system will be reformed in the seven provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Henan, Jiangxi, Hubei, and Fujian first. The stamp tax bureaus for tobacco and liquor in each province have been supervised to investigate the situation and separately reform the special tax for native tobacco. All types of native liquor have now been investigated for their production and sales situation and classified into several categories. According to the fixed tax for liquor promulgated by the Ministry of Industry, if production and sales are within the same province, the tax will be collected in the place of production according to the fixed tax rates. If it is shipped to other provinces for sale and is within the scope of the seven provinces implementing the fixed tax, the fixed tax of the selling province should be paid again when it is transported into the selling province. After the fixed tax has been paid by the producer and seller, within the borders of their respective provinces, in addition to customs duties and liquor and tobacco license taxes, which will still be collected according to regulations, and local surtaxes that were handled before the reform will also be handled temporarily according to the original number and limit of the original actual collection, no other taxes will be levied. The aforementioned tax rates are all calculated based on quantity, without the past malpractices of excessive or insufficient taxation based on value, and can be classified as simple. Merchants and people can easily understand the tax amount payable. It is similar to gradual progress, which can enter into the right track. The procedures for collecting the fixed tax for native liquor have been formulated and promulgated by the Ministry and will be implemented from July 1st of this year. All previously collected public sales fees and taxes will be canceled from the same date. In short, this reform by the Ministry is based on the principle of abolishing excessive harassment and striving for the convenience of merchants and people. All merchants and people should uniformly comply with the new regulations and pay taxes. If they intend to wait and see or obstruct the process, they will be severely investigated. In addition to ordering the stamp tax bureaus for tobacco and liquor in each province to announce the procedures for collecting the fixed tax for native liquor and the newly established fixed tax rates in detail, and to start on schedule, this proclamation is hereby issued.

China National Aviation Corporation Flight 159

to Beijing Returned Due to Fog This Morning

The North China Daily News reports that after the China National Aviation Corporation plane departed from Shanghai at 8:20 a.m. yesterday (the 28th), it flew along the Yangtze River. When it reached 90 miles from Nanjing, it suddenly encountered heavy fog. For safety reasons, the pilot landed the plane on the river. After waiting for 25 minutes, the thick fog began to dissipate. Before taking off, he suddenly felt that the plane was moving slowly. Another pilot urgently inspected the entire plane and saw that the fuselage had cracked and leaked, and water had accumulated to a foot deep. He quickly drained the water, and with the help of passenger Bailey, it took about an hour to drain the water before he could take off again. He then turned back to Shanghai for repairs and arrived at Longhua at 12:30 p.m. Although Bailey experienced this setback, he still plans to take a plane to Jiujiang today (the 29th) and go to Guling for two months to escape the summer heat.

Therefore, there is an initiative to organize an International Aviation Club. Aviators from various countries who come to Shanghai or pass through Shanghai will be hosted by the club. This will not only connect international emotions but also allow Chinese aviators to have the opportunity to contact each other, so as to gain the real benefits of research and improvement.

Company Registration Deadline Extended by Three Months 162

National Federation of Commerce Reissues Circular Telegram

The National Federation of Chambers of Commerce previously received a notice from the Ministry of Industry to inform all companies to apply for registration in accordance with the law. The deadline was the end of June of this year. However, due to transportation obstacles in many places, it was difficult to comply uniformly. Considering the difficulties of merchants, the Ministry of Industry has again notified an extension of three months, from July 1st to September 30th. No further extensions will be granted after the deadline. After receiving the telegram, the Federation of Commerce reissued a circular telegram yesterday. The original text of the telegram is recorded as follows: "To the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce, for the information of all domestic and foreign chambers of commerce: Regarding the case of ordering all companies to apply for registration in accordance with the law, this Federation previously received a notice from the Ministry of Industry, which was forwarded by circular telegram. On June 28th of this year, we again received Notice No. 18509 from the Ministry of Industry, which stated that the deadline for the announcement that all companies should comply with the law and apply for registration was the end of June of this year. The Ministry had already notified this on December 24th of last year and forwarded it to all chambers of commerce for uniform compliance. Many have already complied with the regulations and applied for registration, but there are still many who have not been able to apply for registration by the deadline due to transportation obstacles in the region. In order to consider the difficulties of merchants, the Ministry has specially extended the deadline for another three months, from July 1st to September 30th of this year. It should be known that registration in accordance with the law is of great importance to the legal rights and interests of merchants and people. If companies that have already been established still do not apply for registration by the deadline, the competent authorities in each locality should strictly ban them and investigate them in accordance with the law. In addition to circulating and publishing the notice in newspapers for general knowledge, this notice is sent to the Federation of Commerce, ordering them to instruct all subordinate chambers of commerce to notify all merchants to comply uniformly. The Chairman of the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce, Lin Kanghou, bows, with an official seal."

Requesting the Railway Bureau to Announce Salary Increase Quickly

People Are Anxious, Work Is Unstable, Should Be Announced Quickly

Shenshi News Agency, Shanghai - Because of the routine annual seniority salary increase, the Bureau has not yet announced it this year. They have repeatedly requested the Railways and Railway Authorities to implement it as soon as possible. The Railways and the Railway Bureau have only promised to determine the salary increase standard after performance evaluation. The staff and clerks are dissatisfied and insist on implementing the ordinary seniority salary increase. The original letter is recorded as follows: "Dear Sirs, according to the request of the Executive Committee of the Fourth District Party Headquarters, since the opening of our two railways, the treatment of employees has been quite thorough, and the salary increase of employees is the only hope of our employees. Therefore, employees work hard and do their best to increase their salary and solve the difficulties of life. The workers' salary increase for this year has already been announced, but the staff and clerks' salary increase has not yet been announced, causing the staff and clerks to feel anxious and work uneasily. The staff and clerks and workers of the two railways are like the hands and feet of a human body. Since their obligations are the same, their treatment should also be the same. How can we value one over the other? For the sake of the future of the Railway Bureau and the livelihood of the staff and clerks, it seems necessary to actively resolve the matter. Therefore, it was proposed and discussed at the first plenary session of the Fourth District Representative Congress that a request should be submitted to the special party headquarters to forward it to the Central Committee to order the Ministry of Railways to announce the annual seniority salary increase for the staff and clerks of the two railways in 1933 as soon as possible, so as to expect equal treatment and comfort the public, so that each staff and clerk can work at ease and the future of railway affairs will be more beneficial. The resolution was passed and recorded. We hereby submit the case to your council for review, and we beg you to forward it for the convenience of the party. The Executive Committee of the Special Party Headquarters of the Two Railways, etc. The Sixth District Party Headquarters also submitted a similar request. Accordingly, we hereby send a letter to your Bureau, requesting that you look into the matter and announce the annual seniority salary increase for the staff and clerks of this year as soon as possible. We hope to receive a reply. To the Shanghai-Nanjing-Hangzhou Railway Administration."

Postman Conspired with Two Teenagers 167

Privately Opened Letters Between Young Women

= and drew a turtle on the back of the envelope =

= the postal bureau secretly investigated and filed a lawsuit =

= it concerns obstructing the privacy of others and should be severely punished =

Huang Xuzhu, a Suzhou woman residing at No. 21 Puqing Lane, Malang Road, French Concession, is 16 years old. On the 17th of this month, she had a letter sent to her by her classmate Dai Yaotian from the Liangyou School in Hongkou and delivered to the post office. However, Ye Woyun, a postman from the K'ai-tzu-erh Road postal branch (30 years old, resident of No. 157 Wangzhi Road), delivered the letter to Xu Binglong, a local teenager at No. 7 Cishou Lane, Saporsey Road (20 years old, currently unemployed). Xu opened the letter and read it, then drew a turtle on the back of the envelope and turned the letter over to Huang. After receiving the letter and reading it, Huang did not understand the truth and wrote to Dai Yaotian, blaming him for

not being so playful. 168

After looking at the letter, she turned it over. When Dai received Huang's letter, he was surprised and sent a letter to the post office, requesting an investigation. The bureau sent someone to investigate not only once. It was also learned that on the 14th of this month, a letter sent by Dai Yaotian to Wu Lilian, a woman residing at No. 22 Puqing Lane (Huang's neighbor, same age as Huang, Ningbo native), was also delivered by postman Ye Woyun of the 166 branch office, who first delivered the letter to Qiu Yuansheng, a Ningbo native electrician at No. 11 Kangdi Lane, Kangdi Road (same age as Xu Binglong). After opening the letter and reading it, Qiu then handed it over to Wu. The post office found out the previous situation. Because there was no evidence, it could not be pursued. Therefore, they prepared

letters to Huang and Wu 169

and sent them two identical letters from Dai (test letters). On the afternoon of the 28th (the day before yesterday), they still dispatched the 166 postman to deliver them, and sent patrols Zhu Wenyi and Li Jinlong to secretly follow Ye to investigate. At 3:30, patrol Li Jinlong waited at the entrance of Cishou Lane, Saporsey Road, and saw postman Ye Woyun of the 166 riding a bicycle and delivering the letter to No. 7, handing it over to Xu Binglong and leaving. Li immediately chased to the front of No. 7 to investigate. He happened to see Xu and Qiu holding the letter and opening it to read it next to the cobbler's stall at the entrance of the lane. Li found out the truth and reported it to the bureau. The director reported to the Xiafei Road police station that Xu and Qiu obviously colluded with the postman to

open other people's private letters, 170

which violated the criminal law. The police station sent detectives Ding Wensheng and Guo Bingquan to arrest postman Ye Woyun and Xu and Qiu together and bring them to the eighth criminal court of the court. At 4 p.m., Judge Wu Fanglian took the stand and interrogated them. First, police station lawyer Yuan Jiahan explained the case, and said that the police station was prosecuting the first defendant Ye Woyun for dereliction of duty under Article 138 of the Criminal Code, and the second and third defendants Xu Binglong and Qiu Yuansheng for violating privacy under Article 333 of the Criminal Code, and requested that they be investigated and handled according to law. He also presented four letters. Huang Baohua, a patrolman from the postal bureau, arrived on behalf of the plaintiff, the postal bureau, and stated the previous situation.

Witness Postal Bureau Patrol 171

Li Jinlong testified, "That day, I and another patrolman were at the entrance of Cishou Lane, and saw a postman from the 166 riding a bicycle to deliver a letter. When he entered the lane, we heard someone clapping. Postman Ye Woyun stopped and handed the letter to Xu Binglong inside No. 7. After receiving the letter, Xu returned to his home and came out with Qiu Yuansheng holding the letter. I hurried up and saw that it was a Liangyou envelope. He was opening it next to the cobbler's stall at the entrance of the lane. At that time, someone said that opening other people's private letters was a crime. Qiu replied that it was a letter from my mistress in Hongkou. It doesn't matter to take a look. I immediately returned to the bureau to report." When interrogated, postman Ye Woyun confessed, "I have seen Xu and Huang reading books and talking together before, and Xu told me that he and

Huang are family 172

Xu used to receive letters for Huang before, so I trusted him as family. Xu often told me that if Huang had a letter, I could hand it over to him to forward. That's why I handed Huang's letter to Xu to forward this time. I don't know what else is going on." When questioned, Xu Binglong confessed, "I used to be neighbors with Huang, and we have always been on good terms. She sent me photos and entrusted me to open her letters, so I dared to receive and read the letters for her. I didn't write the turtle on the back." Qiu Yuansheng confessed and denied opening the letter. "When I was repairing the lights in Judge Huang's house in the third special district court, I saw a letter with a turtle on the back, which I drew. I was just joking, but I don't know who sent it to whom, and I didn't have any intention." After repeated cross-examination in court, the defendants' confessions were all evasive and deniable. Finally, Huang and Wu were questioned. According to the confession, although they knew one of Xu and Qiu, they did not entrust them to look at their letters. At this point, the officials began to argue. After the police station lawyer and Ye's lawyer argued, the court declared the debate closed and ordered the defendants to be detained for sentencing on a scheduled date.

National Silk Exhibition Passes Regulations for Soliciting Exhibits 173

丨Chamber of Commerce Petitions Minister of Industry to Come to Shanghai on Time丨

The Chinese National Silk Exhibition, since Vice President Wang Yansong, Preparatory Committee members Zheng Chengqing, and Zhu Boyuan surveyed the venue, has been actively proceeding with the matter of soliciting exhibits. Yesterday, the Preparatory Office held its second meeting and passed items such as the Regulations for Soliciting Exhibits. At the same time, the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce petitioned Minister Chen of the Ministry of Industry to come to Shanghai to attend on time, to show solemnity. The details are recorded as follows:

Preparatory Meeting 174

Yesterday at 4 PM, the Preparatory Office held its second preparatory meeting. Attendees included Chen Jingxuan, Tu Zhongying, Wang Shiqiang, Wang Tai, Bu Boyuan, Zheng Chengqing, Feng Shao, Li Bohang, Ye Weiyi, Luo Fahua, Gao Shiheng, etc., chaired by Director Luo Qinghua. The following resolutions were made: (1) Discussed and passed the budget proposal of the association. (2) Discussed and passed the Regulations for Soliciting Exhibits, the Exhibit Description Form, and the Exhibit Application Form. (3) Decided on the date of the next meeting: a joint meeting of the exhibit solicitation and arrangement groups will be held at 4 PM on July 1st, and the third preparatory meeting will be held at 4 PM on July 2nd.

Regulations for Soliciting Exhibits 175

Regulations for Soliciting Exhibits for the Chinese National Silk Exhibition: Article 1: The Commodity Exhibition Hall of the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce will serve as the exhibit solicitation office. Article 2: The scope of exhibits for this exhibition is limited to domestically produced silk fabrics. Article 3: The types of exhibits for this exhibition include silk fabrics of various colors, damask, silk, gauze, leno, pongee, serge, velvet, and other silk products. Article 4: For the number of exhibits for this exhibition, for the same factory number, if the color and texture of the products are the same, the limit is one to three bolts. Article 5: Exhibitors must fill in the exhibit application form, exhibit description form, and labels made by this association, and indicate any special points separately with concise text. Article 6: This association is scheduled to open on July 9, 1933. Exhibits solicited from various places must be delivered by July 6th, but extensions may be granted with the approval of the Preparatory Office. Article 7: When exhibits are delivered from various places, this association will issue a receipt and be responsible for safekeeping. Article 8: Exhibits will be displayed in showcases and locations designated by this association and will be encouraged accordingly. Article 9: Exhibits may be claimed by exhibitors upon presentation of the receipt one month after the exhibition is full. Those who wish to leave the exhibits for display at the Commodity Exhibition Hall may do so. Article 10: These regulations shall be deliberated and promulgated by the Preparatory Office and implemented.

Exhibit Application Form 176

The content of the exhibit application form is as follows: The undersigned exhibitor hereby wishes to submit the following items to your association for display and agrees to abide by the established rules. This application form is hereby filled out and submitted to the Chinese National Silk Exhibition. Exhibitor's business name and address: Itemized list of product name, trademark, quantity, unit price, total price, and summary.

Exhibit Description 177

Exhibit Description Form for the Chinese National Silk Exhibition: Please fill in the following items: Product name, trademark, place of manufacture, amount of manufacture, manufacturing method, source of raw materials, sales channels, issuing office, distributing office, remarks, exhibitor, business name.

The commodity exhibition hall of the affiliated association will be used as the exhibition venue, and the grand hall will be used as the meeting venue. The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce respectfully bows.

Mediation Process 179

After the dispute occurred, Hong Jianxiang, the municipal commissioner of the district, first took the lead in mediation, but it failed. Later, the Social Affairs Bureau received a report that the weighing merchants, etc., were issued licenses by the Finance Bureau, and their business locations were regulated and could not be moved casually, let alone obstruct the business of the cooperative for no reason. Therefore, it joined forces with the Finance Bureau to send personnel to investigate and ordered the weighing merchants to operate at designated locations. If there were violations or casual movements, the licenses would be revoked.

Police in Huijiao Township Drown a Person While Arresting Gamblers 180

Villagers Who Fell Into the Water Were Threatened and Not Allowed to Come Ashore

If the Police Are So Violent, the Common People Will Have No Way to Survive

A case of police arresting gamblers and causing a drowning in Huijiao, a place in the southwest of this county, has occurred. The details are recorded below. Huijiao is located about three li southwest of Maqiao. To the west of Huijiao is the Yutang Port, to the east is the Dong Yutang River, to the south of the bridge is the border between Songjiang and Suzhou, and to the north of the bridge is the boundary of Shanghai County. It belongs to Yong'an Township in Maqiao District. On the afternoon of the 23rd of this month, at about 4 PM, eight people wearing plain clothes entered the teahouse opened by Jiang Weishi at the north end of Huijiao, claiming that they were police from Maqiao Town and had come to arrest gamblers. At that time, there were three tea drinkers sipping tea. The villagers were all frightened and ran away. At that time, a villager named Zhu Quanlin (40 years old, from Sanyang Township, Minhang First District, Dong Yutang) was washing his feet on the river beach bridge in front of the machine factory next to the teahouse (that is, West Yutang). Those people immediately pointed at Zhu as a gambler and rushed to arrest him. Zhu did not know why he was being arrested. In a moment of desperation, he jumped into the river and swam away, intending to go ashore on the opposite bank. Unexpectedly, those people rushed to the south bank of the river and threatened him with guns, prohibiting him from going ashore. On the north bank, there were also people holding guns and shouting to stop him. Zhu lingered in the river, not allowed to go ashore. Zhu was in a dilemma in the river and extremely anxious. When he swam to the Huijiao pier (about ten zhang from the water bridge), he hugged the wooden stakes under the bridge with both hands and cried for help. (At that time, according to rumors, those people fired two shots, and a person named Hu Huanxiang passed by. Zhu cried out to Huanxiang to save him. When Huanxiang heard the sound and rushed up, he was kicked violently by those people, who said it was none of his business and told him to get out of here quickly. This is noted for now.) At the same time, those people threw bricks and stones at Zhu's head. Zhu was injured and let go, and immediately sank to the bottom of the river and did not float up for a long time. At that time, more and more villagers gathered and, seeing that lives were being lost, they captured those people. At that time, the township chief Zhang Zhongmei heard the news and rushed over. After inquiring, he learned that those people were indeed police from the Sixth District Police Station of Maqiao Town, including officer Zhang Rong and policeman Wang Tiekai. They were not humiliated. There were also patrol leader Xie Fengshan, policemen Jiang En, Wang Lizhang, Xu Enpei, Hua Kegong, Xu Jinhe, and others, a total of six people, who were all angered by the public and tied up with ropes. Because those people were not wearing uniforms and had no symbols (according to the regulations, the township chief should be notified first to avoid misunderstandings), the situation escalated. Xie Fengshan and others were tied up and sent to Sanyang Township, handed over to township chief Nie Shouxian, who escorted them to the Hehangqiao Security Corps overnight before releasing them. (Unexpectedly, the police also beat the escorts.) The next day, they were transferred to the Minhang First District Police Station, and then brought back by Director Zhao of the Maqiao Sixth District. However, after Zhu drowned, Zhang Rong (officer) who caused the trouble, promised to pay for the salvage. Then, at one o'clock that night, he was salvaged with great difficulty and temporarily placed on the river beach south of Huijiao (which is the boundary of Songjiang County). At that time, township chief Wu Yusheng of that place reported to the Songjiang County Government and sent personnel to inspect. At the same time, township chief Nie Shouxian of Sanyang Township reported to the Shanghai Local Prosecutor's Office for inspection. The day before yesterday, prosecutor Wu Deying, commissioned, took prosecutor Xuan Zhiming to the countryside and inspected the body of the deceased Zhu Quanlin, finding a scratch on his forehead and determining that he had drowned. The coroner ordered the family to prepare a coffin for burial pending investigation. Yesterday, the Shanghai County Police Bureau transferred Zhang Rong, Xie Fengshan, Jiang Shouen, Xu Enpei, and Xu Jinhe to the local court for questioning. After a preliminary trial, they were ordered to be detained pending thorough investigation. Moreover, Zhu Huanlin, the brother of the deceased, submitted a statement to the court, stating that the deceased had an 83-year-old mother, as well as a wife and three daughters, and the whole family depended on the deceased for a living. Now, the police abused their power and brutally killed innocent people. On the pretext of arresting gamblers, when people fell into the water, they did not provide assistance but instead forced them to stay ashore. When the younger brother of the civilian was exhausted, he threw huge stones at his head and then shot him with a gun, firing two shots. At this point, my younger brother was physically unable to support himself and was hit so hard that he was swept into the whirlpool and died. The police were originally peacekeepers. When performing their duties, they should wear uniforms and symbols and be peaceful. No matter what kind of criminal behavior, it should not be forced to death. The police were so ignorant and violent. Where is humanity? Where is conscience? The police officers were so barbaric that it showed that the director of the bureau was usually negligent in training and ineffective in managing subordinates. The fault of dereliction of duty is undeniable. If a thorough investigation is not conducted, the good people will have no way to survive in the future, and so on, awaiting instructions.

Public Security Bureau Mediates and Resolves the Situation

After the Social Affairs and Finance Bureaus received the report, they sent personnel to investigate the truth and investigate the instigators yesterday morning at 10 AM. The details are as follows:

Cause of the Dispute 182

Some local enthusiasts in Zhenru District, such as Zhou Dinghua, Shen Zhongyi, Zhou Mucai, Lei Qinfang, Mao Xueyao, etc., in view of the fact that the rural industry in this city was on the verge of bankruptcy after the outbreak of the Shanghai War, specially applied to the Social Affairs Bureau at the end of last year to initiate the organization of the Zhenru District Rural Marketing Cooperative, using cooperative methods to transport and sell agricultural products for farmers. However, the ordinary weighing merchants in the district used various methods against the cooperative.

Large-Scale Electricity Theft Case Concluded 183

=Even the Director of the Investigation Division of the Electric Power Company Was Involved=

=He Leaked the Date of Dispatching Personnel to Copy Electricity Meter Readings in Advance=

丨The Debate Ended Yesterday, and the Verdict Will Be Announced Next Monday丨

Recently, the General Patrol Room cracked a large-scale electricity theft case. Those who participated in the theft work were employees of the Electric Power Company and laid-off workers, who specialized in stealing electricity for various factories and large businesses. For example, if the electricity used by each factory each month was 500 units, the workers would come before the end of the month to destroy the lead seal engraved by the Electric Power Company on the meter, open the meter, and try to reverse the Arabic numerals recording the electricity used, so that 500 units would be changed to 300 units or 200 units. Then, they would close the meter door and affix a forged lead seal. The lead seal was very similar to the one affixed by the Electric Power Company, and it was difficult to distinguish at a glance. Even employees of the Electric Power Company could not detect it. They then shared the remaining profits with the manufacturers. After several months of investigation by Lu Liankui, the Chief Inspector of the General Inspection Office of the Public Concession, the conspiracy was revealed. The thieves Cheng Zhangcai, Zhang Yulin, Liu Zhaoji, Huang Youliang, and Xu Quanlin were arrested. It was found that Xu was currently the Director of the Investigation Division of the Electric Power Company, Zhang and Huang were both workers, Cheng was formerly a worker of the Electric Power Company and had been laid off, and Liu was a coppersmith. Many forged lead seals and a branding iron were seized. It was also found that Cheng and others had committed theft on behalf of dozens of businesses, such as Tianwei Textile Factory on Bailinan Road, Guohua Factory on the same road, Dongfang, Hengfeng, and Youfeng Three Silk Factory on Yulin Road, China Department Store on Nanjing Road, Dahua Department Store, Jiuchun Silk Factory on Hede Road, and Yuandong and Jinya Two Silk Factory on Taopeng Road. Therefore, the Public Concession attorney Ru Baoyi filed a public prosecution against Cheng and the other five people with the First Special Court on charges of theft, forgery of documents, etc., under Articles 338, 340, and 234 of the Criminal Code. Because the Electric Power Company did not want to pursue the matter, the businesses were listed as witnesses. Various aspects of the case have been tried once and have been reported previously. Yesterday, Judge Feng Shide of the Criminal Court held a second hearing. Attorney Ru of the Patrol Room first stated that the defendant Xu Quanling colluded with Cheng Zhangcai to hand over the date table of when the Electric Power Company would dispatch personnel to various users to copy the electricity meter readings to Cheng, so that Cheng could reduce the number of meter readings before the deadline. Cheng benefited, so he gave Xu a certain amount. Therefore, when Cheng was detained, a copy of the above-mentioned form was seized, which was actually given by Xu. When questioned, Xu Quanling denied this fact, only stating that Cheng had asked me about the departure date of the meter readers in February of this year. Because he was a former colleague, I did not suspect anything and told him it was around the fourth or fifth day of the month. I did not expect him to do this. I really did not know. When Cheng Zhangcai was questioned, he took full responsibility, saying that he did this with a certain Zhou and that it had nothing to do with anyone else. Judge Feng then questioned each defendant one by one and then ordered the start of the debate. After Attorney Ru and defense attorneys Fan Gang, Shen Xingxia, Lin Rongqing, Zhang Shewo, Xu Jie, and others debated, the court ordered that the verdict be announced next Monday.

According to the license, and shall not obstruct the business for no reason. Both parties shall not interfere with each other. At the same time, the cooperative side, in order to avoid conflicts, also expressed that it would temporarily operate indoors, and the matter came to an end.

Sudden Strike 184

In recent days, agricultural products are in the peak season. For the sake of their own interests, farmers mostly transport and sell to the cooperative. The business of the weighing merchants has plummeted. Therefore, last Monday, on the pretext that the cooperative's goods were piled up at the entrance, they gathered hooligans to prepare to use force and go on strike to coerce the cooperative to stop operating. After receiving the news, Yao Guangnai, the head of the Fourth District, Third Precinct, believed that the strike by the weighing merchants during the peak season of agricultural products would affect the livelihood of farmers. He immediately took the lead in mediation and persuaded both parties to request instructions from the competent authorities. For the time being, they would continue to operate as usual, and the matter temporarily subsided.

Two Bureaus Investigate 185

After receiving a formal report, the Social Affairs and Finance Bureaus believed that the coercion and strike by the weighing merchants was improper. Therefore, yesterday morning at 10 AM, Hang Ding'an of the Social Affairs Bureau, together with personnel from the Finance Bureau and the Municipal North Inspection Office, went to the site to investigate the actual situation, investigate the instigators, and punish them according to law. They also inquired about everything from the Fourth District, Third Precinct. According to Hang, the weighing merchants should not coerce and strike under any circumstances. Now, after studying the information obtained from the inquiry, the two bureaus will jointly discuss a solution, and the Public Security Bureau will implement it accordingly.

Shen Bao Fourth Edition

Preparatory Committee for Municipal Hospital in Central District Established 187

Articles of Association Passed by the 236th Municipal Meeting

Estimated Expenses Over 500,000 Yuan, Hospital Site Occupies Over 80 Mu

A municipal hospital will be established in the central district of this city, with an estimated cost of over 500,000 yuan and a hospital site occupying approximately 80 mu. In order to complete the project as soon as possible, the municipal government has established a preparatory committee. The rules of the committee have been passed by the 236th municipal meeting and will soon be formed based on the regulations. The articles of association of the preparatory committee for the municipal hospital are copied below.

Organizational Rules of the Preparatory Committee for the Shanghai Municipal Hospital (1) The Shanghai Municipal Government has established the Preparatory Committee for the Shanghai Municipal Hospital (hereinafter referred to as the Committee) in order to prepare for the establishment of a perfect municipal hospital. (2) The Committee shall be in charge of the following matters: (A) Matters relating to the fundraising and management of construction funds. (B) Matters relating to the planning of hospital building construction. (C) Matters relating to the planning of hospital administration and technology. (3) The Committee shall consist of the Secretary-General, the Director of the Health Bureau, the Director of the Finance Bureau, and the Director of the Public Works Bureau as ex officio members, and shall be jointly organized by the Municipal Government by inviting 13 to 19 experts in medicine or architecture and enthusiastic people. (4) The Committee shall mutually elect three standing committee members to handle daily affairs. (5) The Committee shall meet once a month and may hold ad hoc meetings when necessary, all of which shall be convened by the standing committee members. (6) At the Committee meeting, one of the standing committee members shall be mutually elected as chairman. (7) The Committee shall set up the following groups to take charge of affairs: (1) Economic Group, in charge of matters specified in Article 2, Section A of these regulations. (2) Engineering Group, in charge of matters specified in Article 2, Section B of these regulations. (3) Administrative Group, in charge of matters specified in Article 2, Section C of these regulations. (8) Each group of the Committee shall have one director and several staff members, who shall be appointed by the Committee. The Director of the Finance Bureau shall be the Director of the Economic Group, the Director of the Public Works Bureau shall be the Director of the Engineering Group, and the Director of the Health Bureau shall be the Director of the Administrative Group. (9) The rules of procedure for the Committee and the rules of procedure for each group shall be formulated separately. (10) Each group may convene a group meeting, but the matters resolved must be approved by the Committee meeting to take effect. (11) The events decided by the Committee shall be presented by the Committee to the Municipal Government for orders to the competent bureau for implementation. (12) The Committee and each group may borrow incumbent staff from the Municipal Government or the Finance, Public Works, Health, and other bureaus through the standing committee members and group directors to concurrently handle affairs. (13) When necessary, the standing committee members or group directors may notify the section chiefs of relevant bureaus or other relevant personnel to attend the Committee meeting or group meeting to state their opinions. (14) The Committee shall be dissolved after the Municipal Hospital is established, and all its affairs shall be managed by the board of directors organized by the Municipal Government. (15) If these rules are incomplete, they may be amended at any time. (16) These rules shall be implemented from the date of promulgation by the Municipal Government.

Bo Ming's Phonetic Symbols Publicly Tested 189

The Yixing Steamer Arrives in Shanghai for Major Repairs 191

The Yixing steamer of the Jiejiang Company arrived in Shanghai from Yichang on the 24th of this month. When it reached Hankou, due to the impact of severe flooding, it collided with a sea vessel, initially damaging the propeller blades. It then crashed into the outer hull of the midship engine room. Had it not quickly reversed, the Yixing steamer would have been split in two. Fortunately, the Hankou branch dispatched a ship and used cement and wooden planks to patch the damaged areas. It was then towed to Shanghai by the Yiping steamer for major repairs. It arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning. The damage to the steamer is extensive.

Inspecting Soaked Cargo 192

The cargo in the lower hold, all loaded in Chongqing for Shanghai, was entirely soaked by the river water, causing significant water damage. Yesterday morning at 5 AM, the steamer was towed from Yiping to the Huangpu River and docked at the Land Road Biao Mei Wharf to unload the water-damaged cargo destined for Shanghai. The unloading should be completed today. The company will hire a surveyor to inspect the goods and then notify the customers to handle the water damage claims.

Entering the Factory for Major Repairs 193

The damage to the Yixing steamer is extremely serious. Fortunately, the 1,800 bags of wheat on board cushioned the impact of the colliding ship's bow, preventing the entire vessel from being submerged. The passengers had disembarked in Hankou and transferred to another vessel to reach Shanghai. After the Shanghai branch sent personnel to verify the damage yesterday, the steamer will be towed into the Ruirong Shipyard today for major repairs. The total loss is still unknown.

Police Officer Dies Suddenly with Blood from Mouth and Nose 197

| An Autopsy Will Be Performed to Determine the Cause of Death |

Zhang Deyi, a patrolman from the First Precinct of the Southern District, was 39 years old and from Nangong County, Hebei Province. He had been a policeman in the precinct for more than ten years. He had no faults in his daily life. Seven years ago, he cohabited with a woman surnamed Zhang from Jiangbei and lived in Xinhou Zhangjia Alley. They had a son and a daughter, aged six and two respectively. The couple had previously been quite harmonious, but recently they had frequent disputes. At 8:00 PM the night before last, after dinner at home, he went to the police station on duty. At midnight, he was assigned to patrol near the Qinglong Bridge Qinglong Temple when he suddenly clutched his stomach in pain and fell to the ground, unable to get up. Two rickshaw pullers who were sleeping outdoors saw this and came forward to watch. Zhang Deyi's mouth and nose were bleeding, and he was unable to speak. One of them reported it to the police station, and someone sent Zhang to Shanghai Hospital for treatment. By the time the police station received the news and sent someone to investigate, Zhang had died. The time was 1:45 AM. Because the deceased had blood coming from his mouth and nose, and his fingernails were cyanotic, as if he had taken poison, the news was conveyed to his niece-in-law, Zhang Xu (who lived at Wangjia Wharf). According to her, her husband's uncle's death was greatly related to his wife and there had been divorce disputes. She therefore demanded a thorough investigation. The director summoned Qin Defang, the local head of the 23rd Pu, to report to the local court for an autopsy. It is reported that the case will be subjected to an autopsy to clarify the truth.

The Downfall of a Wandering Youth 198

= Overwhelmed by Debt, He Commits Suicide by Taking Poison, and Still Calls a Prostitute for Entertainment Before Death =

Xu Jiafu, from Ningbo, was only in his early twenties. He worked as a clerk at the Zhenfeng Cotton Mill at 33 Henan Road. He was fond of wandering around, so his salary was never enough to cover his expenses, resulting in a mountain of debt that he could not repay. The day before yesterday, after thinking about it, he felt that there was no point in living in the world and decided to end his life. He went to the New Oriental Hotel on Xizang Road alone and booked room 401. He then ordered a bowl of snacks from the tea server. After eating, he still felt lonely, so he summoned a prostitute named Zhao Meiyu to accompany him. That evening, he committed suicide by swallowing opium. At about 6:00 AM the next morning, the woman woke up and saw Xu moaning. She was extremely frightened and ran out to inform the hotel staff, who sent him to Renji Hospital for treatment, but it was ineffective and he soon died. The hospital reported it to the Laozha Police Station, which ordered detective Cao Qishan to investigate. Two suicide notes were found near the deceased's body, stating that he had taken this step due to economic difficulties. The detective then carried the body to the Fellen Road Morgue. Yesterday morning, Guo Wei, a prosecutor from the First Special District Court, came to the morgue to examine the body and ascended to the judge's seat. According to Zhao Meiyu, she was 16 years old. The deceased called her to go there at about 11:00 PM that night. She immediately went to take a bath, but he did not want to. She did not know him and it was their first meeting. She did not know that he had taken opium and committed suicide until she saw his pale face in the morning. According to Wang Zhisun, the deceased was his relative, and his family was all in his hometown. He requested permission to claim the body. After hearing the confession, Mr. Guo ruled that the deceased, Xu Jiafu, had indeed died of opium poisoning. The body was handed over to Wang Zhisun for coffin and burial.

Qiu Dongrong Sentenced for Attempted Murder of His Wife 201

| Sentenced to Five Years in Prison and Ordered to Pay 500 Yuan in Medical Expenses |

Qiu Dongrong, from Guangdong, and his wife, Zeng, had always had a harmonious relationship. Since the January 28th Incident in Shanghai, Qiu joined the 19th Route Army's 61st Division, 183rd Brigade, 364th Regiment, 2nd Battalion, as a quartermaster. When the army set off to Fujian to suppress the communists, Qiu also went with the army. Zeng lived with her in-laws. Recently, because she was repeatedly abused by her in-laws, she had no choice but to seek assistance from the Women's Association. Qiu Dongrong heard about this and left the team on February 20th to come to Shanghai. On June 2nd, he met Zeng at a relative's house at 5 Dade Lane, North Sichuan Road. Qiu invited her to the Dadong Hotel on Yinghua Street and booked room 517. They reconciled for a while. But on the morning of the 3rd, Qiu suddenly had a murderous intent and stabbed her in the head and neck with a knife. She was severely injured. After receiving the report, the Laozha Police Station immediately ordered detective Huang Yingjie to arrest Qiu and send him to the First Special District Court. The police lawyer Ru Baoyi prosecuted him according to Article 284 of the Criminal Code. After the interrogation was concluded, Judge Feng Shide announced the verdict in the First Criminal Court yesterday morning. Qiu Dongrong was found guilty of attempted murder and sentenced to five years in prison, and ordered to pay Qiu Zeng 500 yuan in medical expenses.

Linwu Old Man's Birthday Celebration 204

The great master of the literary world, the old man of Linwu, has lived in Shanghai for more than ten years. He usually expresses his feelings through poetry and songs, listens to music to forget his worries, refuses social gatherings, and does not talk about politics. His high integrity is admired by the people of Shanghai. This summer, in the fifth month, he celebrates his sixtieth birthday. His disciples have all requested to offer congratulations. The old man said that the country is in such a state of disrepair, what is there to celebrate? He firmly refused. His disciples believe that while his wishes should be respected, the celebration cannot be abandoned. It has been decided that on July 6th, at noon, they will gather at Daya Restaurant on Fourth Horse Road to offer birthday toasts. It is expected that the old man will be pleased to see the gathering of his disciples.

The Soy Sauce and Liquor Industry Is Rectifying Market Prices and Is Under Investigation 207

Since the Shanghai Soy Sauce and Liquor Industry Association initiated the rectification of market prices, more than 20 staff members have been working tirelessly in the six districts of Pudong, Nanshi, Zhabei, the British, American, and French districts. Minutes of the Executive Committee Meeting of the National Medical Association 208

The National Medical Association held its 14th Executive Committee meeting of the second session on the 25th. The "attending committee members" Xu Naili, Pang Jingzhou, Yu Yunxiu, Cai Yumen, Jiang Zhenxun, and Wang Qizhang. "Xu substitute" reported. Initially, "Cai substitute" was chaired by Xu Naili, and the following was discussed: (A) Reports (1) Report on the minutes of the 13th Executive Committee meeting in May. (2) Bank balance in February was 2,373.05 yuan. (3) Report on the promulgation of the revised regulations on autopsy of corpses by the Ministry of Health. (4) Report on the publication of the 15th issue of the Medical Bulletin. (B) Discussion (1) The Wuhan Medical Association and the Huaining Medical Association requested the association to submit a request to the National Government to instruct the Ministry of the Interior to extend the period for changing the method of issuing certificates for physician registration for three months (until the end of September this year) in order to universalize it. Resolution: approved. (2) The Nanjing Medical Association stated in a letter that the local government stipulates that the standard of consultation fees should be complied with and requested the association to instruct on the method. Resolution: It is fundamentally wrong for administrative authorities to stipulate physician consultation fees. The association had previously requested the former Ministry of Health to issue an order to all local health administrative agencies nationwide not to stipulate this. The original text was published in the Commentary column of the first issue of the Medical Bulletin and the Correspondence column of the second issue. These documents can be sent to the Nanjing Medical Association for reference. (3) The Jiangdu County Traditional Chinese Medicine Association inquired whether it could restore the name of the Physician Association. Resolution: According to the previous approval No. 147 from the Ministry of Health, "In addition to the term Physician Association in Article 21 of the current Provisional Regulations for Physicians, there are no other regulations." Based on the above approval, reply to the Jiangdu Branch to restore the old name of the Physician Association. (4) The Wu County Medical Association remitted 62.5 yuan from the national disaster medical donation donated by members. How should it be handled? Resolution: The national disaster medical donations shall be disposed of freely by local medical associations, and the remitted donation of 62.5 yuan shall be returned. (5) The Central National Medicine Museum sent a suggestion on the consolidation and unification of disease names and sought opinions. Resolution: Reserved.

Medical Industry 213

Recent News from Guanghua Eye Hospital Guanghua Eye Hospital was established by Dr. Zhang Xiqi, a medical graduate of Chiba Medical College in Japan. Dr. Zhang had previously practiced medicine in Japan and Taiwan and had a distinguished reputation. Due to the oppression of the Japanese invaders, he returned to China in 1910 and practiced medicine in the west end of the Xiaocai Market in Baxianqiao. Over the years, he has cured countless patients with eye diseases, and as a result, those who come from all directions seeking medical treatment are almost overwhelmed. In response to the requests of patients, Dr. Zhang has greatly expanded the hospital. It is reported that the hospital can specially consider the situation of the poor and reduce medical expenses.

Yangsi Epidemic Hospital Opens Last year, a severe epidemic caused disaster, and the Yangsi District of Pudong suffered the most. Fortunately, two gentlemen from Pudong, Chen Zixin and Zhang Shangyi, discussed with Dr. Wang Zhenchuan and raised funds to establish an epidemic hospital. After three months of opening, the results were remarkable and the reputation was widely praised. At present, the summer heat is high and the epidemic demon is on the rise. In addition to undertaking economic affairs, Chen and Zhang continue to invite Dr. Wang Zhenchuan, the president of the Jishan Hospital, to serve as the president and take charge of all medical affairs. At present, preparations have been completed and the opening is scheduled for July 1st. Dr. Wang has served in the Red Cross for many years and is not only highly skilled in medicine, but also has rich experience in epidemics and emergencies.

Zhejiang Province Education Bureau Alters Examination Procedures for Education Expenses in Various Counties 220

Chen Bulei, Director of the Zhejiang Education Bureau, noted that the educational expense budgets of various counties in the province are currently prepared by the county education bureaus and submitted to the county education bureau's education committee for deliberation and passage. They are then reviewed and approved by the county administrative meeting before being forwarded for examination. However, to ensure the overall budget is taken into account, it is proposed that the approval procedure be slightly modified. The "Procedures for the Compilation and Examination of Local Educational Expense Budgets in Various Counties" were drafted and passed by the Provincial Government at its 584th meeting. The measures are as follows: (1) The local educational expense budgets of various counties shall still be forwarded by the county governments to the Education Bureau for examination, as per the existing practice, and shall also be incorporated into the county's overall budget. However, the county administrative meeting will no longer review this item. (2) The Education Bureau will send its examination opinions to the Finance Bureau for joint review, after which orders will be issued to the counties for compliance.

Local News 225

The Municipal Education Bureau Restricts the Establishment of Middle Schools

There are Already Many General Middle Schools in this City

There is Truly No Need to Establish More

The Municipal Education Bureau has previously received an order from the Ministry of Education restricting the establishment of general middle schools, which has already been recorded and announced. The original text is as follows: "In accordance with the order from the Ministry of Education, briefly stating, 'Restricting the establishment of general middle schools, the Ministry has repeatedly ordered compliance. There are already many general middle schools in Shanghai, and there is truly no need to establish more. In the future, if there are requests to establish secondary schools, they should be ordered to properly raise funds and establish vocational schools to meet the needs,' etc." Therefore, the case of restricting the establishment of general middle schools has already been recorded and announced by this Bureau. Now, in accordance with the order from the Ministry of Education restricting the establishment of general middle schools and encouraging the opening of vocational schools, in the future, all those opening secondary schools should immediately comply with the Ministry of Education's directive to properly raise funds and establish vocational schools, otherwise, approval will not be granted. This order is hereby issued for your information.

During the Holidays, Children Should Be Sent to the Bureau for Free Dental Treatment

The Health and Education Bureaus jointly issued a letter to parents yesterday regarding children's dental health. The original letter reads: "Dear Sir/Madam, for the purpose of promoting children's dental health, this Bureau, etc., has specially established a dental clinic within the Education Bureau to provide free treatment to students from various schools who have dental defects, accompanied by their teachers. As the summer vacation for various schools is now in progress, your parents can take advantage of the vacation to continue treatment for your children, in order to restore their health as soon as possible and avoid wasting their studies during normal school hours. Accordingly, you are notified to request treatment record cards from the school authorities and escort your children to the clinic for treatment. The examination hours are from 8:00 AM to 4:00 PM every day, and from 8:00 AM to 12:00 PM on Saturdays. Closed on Sundays. Students in the Gaogqiao District should still go to the Gaogqiao Township Health Office of the Health Bureau for treatment."

Li Shizeng, et al. Host a Lecture by Martin

The Geneva Chinese International Library's Shanghai Office has been collecting books for several months. Many people from all walks of life have responded and donated. Names of Attendees: The attendees yesterday included Martin, Chu Minyi, Zhang Gongquan, Xie Shou Kang, Liu Zhanen, Wang Xiaolai, Guo Dehua, Xu Xinliu, Su, Hualin, Ying Shi, Wang Yaxuan, Fang Fuan, and other Chinese and foreign guests, totaling more than two hundred people, hosted by Li Shizeng and the staff of the World Society.

Book Display: After arriving, the guests successively visited the books of the International Library, which were displayed separately in various rooms on the second and third floors. Most of them were ancient books, especially in the history section. The new books published by various publishing organizations were displayed in a corner on the third floor. According to the office staff, the collected books have reached six-tenths of the modern national publications and will continue to be sought to ensure that nothing is missed. In addition to sending the books to Geneva, a branch library will be set up in Shanghai for reference, they said. After the visit, they took photos in the lawn in front of the house and then went to the hall for the tea party.

Martin's Lecture: At 5:20 PM, Li Shizeng introduced Martin to the stage to give a lecture. Martin's topic was "The Swiss Federal System and China." After giving the lecture in French, it was translated by Shen Liang. The general idea was that Switzerland has the smallest land area in the world, while China has the largest land area. It seems that there is absolutely nothing in common between the two. However, if we study it carefully, the two countries, one large and one small, have many similarities. For example, the language and writing in Switzerland are in French and German, which are very inconsistent. Although Chinese characters are unified, the languages ​​are different in various places. In addition, although the Swiss territory is small, its complexity is not inferior to China. Therefore, the Swiss political system can be used for China to learn from. It lasted for more than an hour before it ended.

National Music Performance: After Martin's speech, the Datong Music Society played national music. First, Wu Zhaolan played the guqin "Stone Spring", followed by Wei Zhongle playing the pipa "Huaiyin Pingchu", the tempo was fast and slow, Ma Jiong's drums sounded, as if in a battlefield. Finally, the National Music Association played three chapters of the Great National Music and dispersed, when the clock struck seven o'clock. After the meeting, according to Guo Dehua, Martin will have a banquet tomorrow, and he is expected to return to Europe in four or five days.

Summer Health Patrol Lecture at the Civic Education Center 229

The Gaogiao and Caohejing Districts Have Been Held Separately

The Third Tour Will Be in the South Shanghai District Next Thursday

The Shanghai Municipal Civic Education Center held a Summer Health Patrol Lecture in various districts to expand the promotion of summer health and increase public health knowledge. The two districts of Gaogqiao and Caohejing were held separately on the 21st and 25th of this month. The grand occasions are recorded as follows:

The first summer health patrol lecture in the Gaogqiao District was held in the Gaogqiao Chenghuang Temple. In advance, the museum liaised with the Gaogqiao Health Branch and the Gaogqiao Primary School to discuss the venue and layout matters. Therefore, the opening was very calm, and the students of Gaogqiao Primary School wrote slogans and added performances, which was commendable. The meeting opened at 1:00 PM, and people came to listen in an endless stream, with an estimated total of more than 1,000 people. Local schools and the Public Security and Health Branch also sent personnel to participate. First, the staff of the museum gave a popular health lecture and distributed summer medicines. The tour then performed various entertainment programs, including dances and health songs. Finally, there was a costume speech, a play titled "Incorrigibly Foolish," which was wonderful and well received by the public.

The second tour lecture in the Caohejing District was held in the Caohejing Qiuzhi Primary School. Staff were sent in advance to properly arrange the layout, and the order was well organized. The meeting opened at 1:00 PM. However, because there were fewer listeners, the costume parade was changed to a week on the streets, and the number of people suddenly increased, making it extremely crowded, with about 1,200 people. At that time, the costume speech "Incorrigibly Foolish" was performed, and music was played, and the national martial arts class of the museum performed fighting skills, with broadswords and axes, which was appreciated by the audience. It is reported that the third patrol lecture has been scheduled to be held in the Shanghai South District Civilian Residence next Thursday, and there will be a grand occasion at that time.

Liang Shi-Yi Scholarship for Subsidy Students 235

Two Students Each from Agriculture, Industry, and Commerce Departments

Annual Subsidy of 400 Yuan

Liang Shi-Yi, together with the Academic Assistance Committee, in order to assist Qingchao (Qing Dynasty) descendants to enter universities, will start the first session this autumn. Six subsidy quotas will be set, designated as two for the Agricultural Department of Lingnan University in Guangzhou, two for the Industrial Department of Jiaotong University in Shanghai, and two for the Commerce Department of Nankai University in Tianjin. Each student will receive a tuition subsidy of 400 national currency yuan per year from the association, paid in two installments, until graduation from university. Applicants must be graduates of public and registered senior middle schools, with excellent grades but unable to afford further education. Registration locations are at the aforementioned three universities.

Wimbledon, Day Three 242

Another Unexpected Event in the World Tennis Tournament

▲American Doubles Champion Barnes Imitates Gran Gale

▲Loses to Australian Quist and Turnbull Team

▲Singles British Lees Defeats McCrath

(London, 28th) Two surprising results occurred in this afternoon's Wimbledon tennis match, described as follows:

▲American Doubles Championship Failure

In the first week of the men's doubles, the South Australian youth players Quist and Turnbull defeated the American doubles champions Barnes and Gran Gale with a surprising performance. The American players won the first two sets, but afterwards, they were at a loss. Their opponents were full of energy and defeated them with fierce attacks. In the end, they lost three sets in a row, only getting eight games. Quist and Turnbull won 4-6, 5-7, 6-2, 6-4, 6-2.

▲Lees Defeats McCrath

In another match, the 17-year-old Australian youth McCrath was defeated by the British Davis Cup player Lees. The score was a straight three sets. Lees won easily with 6-4, 6-3, 6-1. Lees's shots were sharp and accurate. Although the 17-year-old Australian youth used the special skill of double-handed backhand to counterattack from time to time, it was not enough to stop the opponent's fierce attacks. It is unexpected that McCrath, who defeated the top Japanese player Sato in the Davis Cup rematch, lost to Lees in a straight three sets this time.

▲Results of Other Singles Groups

In addition to the Lees vs. McCrath group, the results of the other men's singles groups are as follows: (1) Cochern (France) defeated Bo Hui'er (USA) 2-6, 6-4, 6-3, 5-7, 6-3; (2) Stetmen (New Zealand) defeated Condon (South Africa) 9-11, 6-3, 6-2, 5-7, 6-4; (3) Crawford (Australia) defeated Qin Ding (France) 6-3, 6-4, (8-6; (4) Sato (Japan) defeated Lesett (England) 4-6, 6-3, 6-0, 6-2; (5) Hughes (England) defeated Aoki (Japan) 6-2, 6-1, 6-0.

▲Preliminary Results of Men's Doubles

The first week of the men's doubles competition began today. Stokefen and Sed (USA) defeated Blancnet and Morin (France) 6-3, 2-6, 9-7, 6-4. Gregory and Whittle (England) defeated Ito and Miki (Japan) 6-2, 6-0, 8-10, 6-1.

▲Second Week of Women's Singles

The results of the second week of the women's singles competition are as follows: (1) Natt Ho (England) defeated Toms (England) 6-4, 6-2; (2) Skriver (England) defeated Jia Fuli (England) 6-2, 1-6, 6-3 (3) Sted Maus (England) defeated Shi Qu Lauxun 6-3, 6-3; (4) Enfeibrujie (Germany) defeated La Ais (USA) 6-4, 6-4. In the third week, Horne (Germany) defeated Ya Liyawusi Jia (Poland) 6-3, 6-3.

▲Second Week of Mixed Doubles

In the second week of the mixed doubles, Mrs. Helen Whels Madi and Xu Shi defeated A Fulei and Ms. Shi Quleixun, with a score of 6-2, 6-3, very easily.

Renovation of Takahashi Swimming 246

Among the seaside beaches, only Takahashi exists in Shanghai. Promoted by the municipal authorities last year, it once stirred things up. However, all the equipment was temporary in nature. Therefore, there was a lack of places to eat and drink. If there was unexpected weather, it was difficult to find a place to shelter from the rain. The most unpleasant thing was that there was no fresh water to rinse the body after bathing, which felt dirty and uncomfortable. Moreover, when the tide was low, the water was only head-high thirty to forty miles away from the beach, a muddy yellow, and there were no facilities, which made the learners uninterested, and the good swimmers had no place to show their heroism. Now, local gentry, Zhang Peigen and Zhao Fuji, etc., are building a magnificent seaside hotel for the sake of people in this city to cool off and swim. Facing the ocean, the cool breeze is pleasant, the layout is exquisite, and the equipment is complete. In the future, tourists will not have to travel six miles to Takahashi Town for a full meal. A few days ago, swimming experts from Shanghai, such as Yu Binqi and Wang Jianxin, were invited to Takahashi for consultation on the necessary equipment for swimming, such as water depth markers, relay buoys, ten rowing boats, to accompany long-distance swimmers to exert their power as much as possible, bamboo poles, and galvanized iron buckets were prepared for beginners to float, and there were also lifeboats and other insurance to make the swimmers happy and clean. The neat tents and fresh water were all available. In addition, the high tide this year has made things even better. It is said that it will open on the ninth of next month.
